"Lucky for me, I have grasped the skill of creating the Cold Prison. If not, I might have died in your cat's stomach. But unfortunately for youâ€¦"

As he was still speaking, Lamont stretched out a finger and aimed at King Ieuan below. A white aura began circling on his fingertip. An extreme murderous intent was oozing in his eyes.

Swoosh! A blast of cold air was condensed into a white arrow. It quickly darted off from Lamont's finger and dashed towards King Ieuan.

King Ieuan just stared at the approaching arrow, as if fear and helplessness crippled its entire body.

"My king, get a hold of yourself!"

"You need to run!"

Oakley, Dempsey, and the three other Ear Mice rushed over to King Ieuan as fast as they could.

The five Ear Mice were King Ieuan's most trusted subordinates. Even in the most hopeless situation, their loyalty and passion to protect their king remained undaunted.

"Divine Picture Shield!"

Suddenly, a round purple shield appeared above Oakley's head.

Aside from the Heaven Shaking Gold, the Divine Picture Shield was its most powerful Other Shore Token.

It was a defense-type Other Shore Token from Stage Thirty-three. The power of any kind of attack that came in contact with it would automatically be reduced to one-third of its original strength.

With this, even if Lamont was a high-level Eternal Realm master, Oakley was confident that it would withstand his attack.

Whoosh! Oakley's eyes widened as it saw that the white arrow pierced through the Divine Picture Shield. It didn't stop for one bit, and it drilled into Oakley's chest. Immediately after, Oakley became frozen like an ice sculpture.

Seeing what happened, Dempsey, who was behind Oakley, immediately threw an Interchange Stone Tablet towards the white arrow. The moment it latched onto the arrow, Dempsey activated the stone tablets.

In the blink of an eye, the white arrow disappeared and re-appeared in another direction where it pierced into another huge piece of rock.

The rock that came into contact with the arrow became brittle and instantly shattered into a pile of ice dregs.

King Ieuan came back to its senses and was astonished at Oakley's sudden death. Its face was quickly filled with grief and anger. It abruptly took out two Other Shore Tokens, which were a pair of sharp and shiny knives.

The light reflecting on the knives left countless deep cuts on the surface of the surrounding rubbles.

King Ieuan knew that in one way or another, it was going to be killed by Lamont. So, it chose to fight until death rather than try to escape like a pathetic king.

"Tch. Do you think your bravery will gain you anything? You useless rodent!"

Lamont had no intention of taking King Ieuan seriously. So, he raised his hand and decided to kill the latter in a swift manner.

Just then, several golden light blades came rushing from a distance and rained on Lamont.

Swoosh! Crash! The moment the light blades fell into the Cold Prison, they instantly turned into countless dots of light that eventually vanished.

Standing on the Panoramic View Peak, Yan glared at Lamont with tremendous hostility.

Zen knew the secret of the Cold Prison, and he also knew that at the current level of the Energy Shaft, it would be useless and too weak to break the Cold Prison, let alone damage Lamont.

However, he didn't expect that Yan would suddenly make a move, so he had no time to stop her.

Lamont was initially focused on dealing with King Ieuan, but after Yan's sudden attack, she successfully attracted his attention.

"Human girl, I'd like to commend you for your courage."

Lamont turned towards Yan with a huge ugly smile on his gorilla-like face.

Immediately after, his huge body rushed towards her.

Whoosh! Yan quickly unleashed the golden shield again.

With the efforts of the Ear Mice, the energy of the Cloud Cover Array was replenished to such an extent that the golden shield was quite solid.

Then, Lamont stretched out a finger. In an instant, the shield turned into dots of light and immediately dissipated.

Lamont let out a horrifying laugh. He quickly clenched his fist and attempted to throw a massive punch directed at Yan.

As his fist was approaching her, the Cold Prison touched Yan and dispersed her energy.

She didn't disappear but was transformed into a form under the extremely low temperature. It was actually very similar to the form outside of the chaos.

"B-brotherâ€¦"

As her consciousness was slowly fading, her instinct made her call for Zen.

Suddenly, Zen's body expanded as he activated his Wild God Body.

The truth was he didn't want to fight any Chaos Ancient God right now.

Before he had mastered the ancestry-level bloodline, his strength was just comparable to that of an ordinary Eternal Realm warrior.

However, he didn't have much choice right now. In the face of the overwhelming odds, he had to bite the bullet.

In addition to unleashing his own strength, he could only bet on the power of the ancestry-level bloodline.

"I hope you can be smart enough to know what you are doing!"

In a flash, Zen's body expanded to a height of more than four million feet, like a huge mountain, protecting Yan at all costs.

Lamont was over ten million feet tall, so Zen was just half of his size.

As Lamont threw the punch towards Yan, he clearly saw how Zen turned into a giant. A smile crossed his ferocious face and his expression became more intense.

'Come to think of it, is this the guy that Herbert mentioned? They said that they will be capturing him alive.

Ha-ha, they can't blame me. He's the one who walks into his death, ' Lamont thought.

Even Lamont couldn't fully control the Cold Prison. Anything that came in contact with it would be ripped off its energy, and Lamont couldn't restore them either. Trying to protect Yan, Zen rushed into the Cold Prison and approached Lamont's fist by throwing his own massive punch. Lamont couldn't help laughing in his mind because he knew that Zen already fell into the trap, and he would surely end up like the others who became victims of the Cold Prison.

However, Lamont's expression suddenly changed and his eyes widened.

Crash! With a muffled sound, Zen's fist collided with Lamont's. Zen wasn't stopped by the Cold Prison and his energy didn't dissipate either.

Due to the overwhelming force that Zen had put in his fist, Lamont was pushed back and had to take several steps backward.

Lamont's force was undoubtedly more powerful than Zen's. However, he didn't use his full strength just now because he didn't expect that it would be necessary.

As Lamont regained his balance, he stared at Zen with a visibly disorganized expression on his face. He was trying to understand what had just happened. He was thinking if Zen used a certain secret skill that he missed to notice.

"This can't beâ€¦ You! What the hell did you do?"

Lamont knew very well how the Cold Prison worked, so he was flabbergasted at what just happened.

"What? You're wondering why the Cold Prison didn't work on me?" Zen looked at his slightly stiff fist and brushed off the frost on its surface. "Well, your Cold Prison is only so-so."

Chapter 3918 Strengthen The Cold Prisons in the Blooming Jade Stage were forbidden lands for any creature, and even Zen didn't dare to enter.

Only those who were as supernormal as Pompeo could stay in a Cold Prison.

The Cold Prison had an extremely low temperature. What made it more terrible was that the creatures of the chaos seemed to slowly turn into light dots and then vanish into thin air inside it.

Yet for the creatures of the Abstruse Energy World, the Cold Prison was not so dreadful. Even some relatively weak creatures of the Abstruse Energy World would only be temporarily frozen when they fell into it. Once they left the Cold Prison, they would recover from frozen state, and again return to being energized and vigorous.

Zen had decided to take action because he was worried about Yan.

Although the ancestry-level bloodline could defeat all the energy, the Cold Prison was very special. It could be possible that Zen himself might be destroyed in it.

The moment he came into contact with the Cold Prison, the temperature began to rise unexpectedly. Zen felt it was easily breakable.

"You know this is the Cold Prison? And you are able to break it?" Lamont finally uttered, after a moment of silence.

"There are many Cold Prisons in the Blooming Jade Stage." Zen smiled. As to whether he could break it or not, he didn't need to answer.

Lamont carefully looked at Zen. He had been thinking about whether he should kill him earlier. "It seems that I thought too much. I'm afraid it will take me a lot of energy to defeat you!"

Swoosh...

Lamont tilted his huge body and pounced towards Zen.

He was an old monster that had lived for countless years. His eyes were extremely sharp and he possessed great knowledge.

Indeed, Zen had an incredible method to break the Cold Prison. Even Lamont was convinced that he was capable.

However, he also sensed that Zen's strength was not enough. Lamont's physical body was an advantage; it was no doubt that he could overthrow Zen! When Lamont went to face Zen, a red light flashed from Yan's eyes. Golden light blades appeared, moving in cutting motions towards his head.

Lamont, having suffered from a loss once, drew a huge ice cover enclosing Yan's head. He then grabbed Zen in midair, and ruthlessly smashed him towards the Pear Hill.

Boom! Boom! Zen's more than four million-foot-tall body crashed into a mountain. The impact embedded his body onto the Pear Hill.

The originally solid and huge mountain crumbled, almost becoming as soft as mud; it was unable to bear the damage of two giant creatures.

Whoosh! A ray of white light flashed from Lamont's hand. A long and thin ice spike started to form and stabbed towards Zen's head.

Zen had no time to dodge and instead reached out his hand to grab the ice spike.

As the ancestry-level bloodline started a surge within Zen's body, the ice spike appeared to have been roasted and instantly melted into a pool of water.

Lamont was stunned again. He frowned as he refused to use the power of truth any longer. He simply drew his fist back and powerfully punched Zen! Boom! Boom! Boom! The sudden vibration reverberated throughout the whole Pear Hill.

The scene wasn't new for many people in the Pear Hill; but the mountain leaders, the sect leaders, the disciples, and the members of the race were unable to participate in such a level of battle. On the other hand, they needed to provide Yan with a steady flow of energy.

Crack! Yan had finally smashed the ice cover on her head into little pieces. She looked for her brother, but when she saw him, her eyes turned red. He was being pressed and attacked on the ground! Buzz...

The Energy Shaft began to shake violently.

The energy gained through the Cloud Cover Array had been released by Yan.

With the help of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization, the energy that the Energy Shaft could transform had greatly increased, but there was still a limit.

The energy released by Yan exceeded this limit! Clatter, clatter, clatter...

The huge golden blades spiraled at high speed and flew to hit Lamont.

Overpowered by the golden blades, he immediately employed the Cold Prison again.

The Cold Prison didn't have any effect on Zen, but it could entirely restrain Yan's energy attack.

Without sound, light or vibration, the several huge golden light blades entered the Cold Prison and turned into tens of millions of white light dots before dissipating.

Yan's chest heaved up and down while her face flushed into a strange red.

This kind of energy overuse did great damage to her. Shortly, she became unable to use the Energy Shaft. She could only watch in agony as Lamont kept beating up Zen's body.

Previously, during Zen's communication with the ancestry-level bloodline, the ancestry-level bloodline had massively strengthened him.

However, this strengthening was limited, and was unable to block Lamont's attack.

After the Chaotic Source Spirits fell into fatigue, wounds and injuries began to cover Zen's body. Besides his control of the temperature, Lamont's physical quality also made him become outstanding among the Chaos Ancient Gods.

At this time, Zen could resist if he used a Civilization Artifact's Inheritance of World. He remembered that the Primeval Lord of Heaven had given him the suggestion.

But this suggestion was rejected by Zen. Even if he activated the Inheritance of World, he might still not be a match for Lamont. After all, Lamont was skilled in dealing with the attacks of energy.

He wanted to take advantage of this opportunity to continue convening the ancestry-level bloodline to come to his aid.

Boom! Boom! Boom! Boom...

Lamont attacked like a huge gorilla, his thick hands punching on Zen's body. Zen's chest bones cracked as they were broken into pieces.

While Lamont was still launching his constant attacks, a slight confusion struck him.

He felt that although Zen's strength was very weak, he wasn't likely to have given up struggling.

He looked at Zen closely and wondered why under his body, Zen seemed to have stopped resisting.

'What's going on?' Before Lamont could figure it out, something more strange happened. Zen began talking to himself.

"Aren't you afraid of being in another person's hands? If I lose, your situation will become worse! I don't think they will let you go. You're wasting your only chance!"

According to the information from the brush-wielder and the four statues, Zen was the only one who had fused with the complete ancestry-level bloodline and was able to take it away. No one had ever done that before.

Zen's communication with the ancestry-level bloodline distracted Lamont.

Although he didn't stop punching, the agitation in his eyes was evident. It grew stronger and stronger as Zen continued to talk.

Who was he trying to persuade? Was he trying to convince someone who could finish Lamont? Zen's chest suddenly cracked...

Surprisingly, no blood flowed as his broken ribs were exposed, extending to both sides.

The texture of the broken ribs quickly changed and the ribs like two rows of blades directed towards Lamont.

The abrupt transformation broke off Lamont's attack. He felt an instinctive threat.

If he didn't kill this brat, something unexpected would happen! "Go to hell!" he shouted.

He used up all his strength and smashed towards Zen's head.

Zen's eyes, mouth, and nose sank, revealing a horrifying appearance. His face was deformed.

As Lamont hit hard, his fist sunk deep into Zen's head with a sunken face.

Out of instinct, Lamont tried to pull his fist back, but he failed.

Chapter 3919 Helpless Zen's head remained latched onto Lamont's hand as if he was biting into it.

Then, Lamont raised his arm and lifted Zen's body with it.

"Let go of me, you bastard!"

Lamont swiftly swung his arm sideways in an attempt to throw Zen into the Pear Hill.

However, Zen remained firmly latched onto his hand. Even though Lamont was knowledgeable and powerful, a strong sensation of anxiety and vexation was creeping beneath his skin.

Since Zen wouldn't let go, Lamont raised him high in the sky and smashed him down to the mountain.

Unexpectedly, Lamont didn't feel that Zen was loosening his grip, so he smashed him again and again.

In just a few seconds, several craters appeared on the top area of Pear Hill where Lamont repeatedly smashed Zen's body.

However, even though Lamont felt that he almost used up all his strength, his hand was still unable to get rid of Zen.

Yan grew worried and speechless as she saw her brother being beaten so furiously.

Zen seemed to withstand all of Lamont's attacks, but it wouldn't be good for him to be continuously beaten like this.

Crash! Crash! Crash! As Zen was still being rammed into the Pear Hill, a huge stone about ten feet wide flew towards the side and almost hit King Ieuan, who had just climbed out of the Pear Hill.

Crack! Before the huge chunk of stone hit King Ieuan, its tail whipped the stone at high speed, splitting it into two halves.

The other Ear Mice also followed King Ieuan and had a clear view of the brutal battle between Lamont and Zen. However, as they watched intently, there was a strange sensation that they couldn't shake off.

Zen was a dear friend of the Ear Mouse race. All of the members present, including King Ieuan, knew all of the miraculous things that he did in the past.

They never even thought that Zen could already fight the Chaos Ancient God after he got out of the Eternal Scroll Painting.

"I don't understand what's happening. Zen's current state is pretty strange.

He seems to be seriously injured now, but he can still latch onto Lamont,"

an Ear Mouse told its observation.

King Ieuan nodded at the Ear Mouse's statement and stared at Zen with its soybean-sized eyes. "His body has indeed become very strange. I don't think he is injured. It's as if his body voluntarily became like this..."

"Does that mean that his bloodline affects his physical body this way?" one of the Ear Mice blurted as it was lost in thought. Actually, it was not that unusual for an Eternal Realm warrior to obtain some kind of bloodline that could alter their physical body.

However, King Ieuan explained further, "That's not exactly the point. Did you notice that for a while now, Lamont hasn't used his bloodline power? That's the most exceptional thing so far! Zen might've done something that we couldn't comprehend."

The greatest reliance of Chaos Ancient Gods was their bloodline power, which was known as the truth-level theurgy. This was their basic foundation.

However, when the power of truth became ineffective, they could only rely on their sturdy physical body.

Bang! Bang! After launching several consecutive attacks, Lamont finally had enough of it. He grabbed the air with his other hand and summoned a huge ice blade that was formed by thick white mists.

At the back of Lamont's mind, he thought that since Zen had degenerated into this pitiful form, it would be impossible for him to resist his power of truth again.

As the ice blade slashed towards Zen, Zen's strange body didn't react to it and just continued latching himself on Lamont's hand.

However, just as the ice blade was about to touch Zen, one of his hands quickly responded.

It seemed to have an extreme ability of perception, like having an eye of its own. His hand accurately held off the sharp edge of the blade and the blade didn't even cut him.

Immediately after, the sharp ice blade melted completely.

Then, his hand quickly went back.

Lamont felt like he was going insane.

He couldn't get rid of Zen or smash him to death. Moreover, his theurgy was being completely suppressed. There was nothing left that he could do to beat him.

The current situation was something new to Lamont and that was why he was very frustrated.

Lamont never had the intention to take Zen seriously before, but now, he couldn't believe that he would become so troublesome.

"What the hell is wrong with you? Why can't you die?"

Lamont was so exasperated now. He wanted to finish this useless battle as soon as possible, so he began dragging Zen to a mountain nearby.

The peak was like a sharp sword that was soaring into the sky. It turned out to be the Sword Blade Peak, which was apparently guarded by the mountain leader, Dwight Xu.

While on the mountain, Dwight Xu was also silently observing the vicious battle between Zen and Lamont. Upon seeing that the two were headed towards the mountain, he immediately gave an order to all the disciples stationed there.

"All disciples must retreat from the Sword Blade Peak at once!"

There were several mountains around the Pear Hill.

In previous battles, the disciples in the mountains naturally felt their power.

However, even if they tried their best to release their energy, the strong feeling of fear was still there.

After all, it was a Chaos Ancient God that Zen was dealing with. If they were slightly affected, it might cost them their lives.

Therefore, as soon as Dwight Xu gave the order to retreat, all the disciples hurriedly used the Grand Teleportation technique and dispersed in all directions.

Just a moment ago, there were tens of thousands of people on the Sword Blade Peak, but now, it was completely empty.

Lamont dashed in front of the Sword Blade Peak and stopped there. Then, he stretched his hand to pat the peak.

Gradually, as Lamont continued to put his palm on the peak, the Sword Blade Peak became frozen solid and almost impregnable.

Even Fuxi and the Snake Goddess would have a hard time destroying it.

After freezing the peak, Lamont dragged Zen and made a giant leap into the sky.

Upon seeing his course of action, King Ieuan, Yan, Dwight Xu, and the others immediately understood what he was trying to do.

Lamont brought Zen up in the sky and wanted to impale him straight into the Sword Blade Peak.

Right now, this was the best idea that Lamont had thought. He didn't have any other good way to kill Zen on his current state.

Zen might not be able to eliminate Lamont's power of truth, if his physical body fell down at high speed. He would be defeated once his body was successfully impaled through the Sword Blade Peak.

However, just as Lamont aggressively dragged Zen up in the sky, one of Zen's arms suddenly stretched downward and extended as if it had lost all of its bones. It patted the Sword Blade Peak and injected a stream of green energy into it.

Sizzle! The Sword Blade Peak, which was frozen solid just seconds ago, instantly melted. Not only that, the surface of the mountain blossomed into what seemed to be a fairyland, full of various plants all around.

Lamont's jaw dropped while he was still in midair. Obviously, he was shocked at what just happened.

Even the others who saw the scene were utterly surprised.

"Zen, what is this?"

Yan couldn't believe her eyes. "Is this even a battle?"

Zen, a superior human being, and Lamont, a powerful Chaos Ancient God, were two of the most powerful beings in the entire chaos because of their abilities and strength.

But right now, the battle between these two mighty beings was not making any sense.

Lamont stayed in midair for a few more seconds, and then decided to go back down at the Sword Blade Peak. He patted the peak again and infused the power of truth into it.

After quite some time, Lamont noticed that the Sword Blade Peak wasn't freezing.

As he lowered his head, Lamont saw Zen's slender and boneless hand was also touching the mountain, countering the effect of his power of truth.

"Ha-ha! What the hell!"

In the distance, Dwight Xu couldn't help but burst out laughing.

King Ieuan and the other Ear Mice on the other side of Pear Hill also laughed out loud.

Even Yan temporarily forgot that her brother was in danger. She just couldn't believe that a vicious battle would turn into a comedy show.

"You bastard!"

Lamont felt that he was going crazy. His angry roar echoed throughout the entire Pear Hill.

Ten minutes...

Fifteen minutes...

With what had happened just now, his bodily transformations didn't surprise him anymore.

The ancestry-level bloodline could completely change the shape of one's body. Even if part of his body had been assimilated after he devoured Lamont, the ancestry-level bloodline should've been able to quickly repair it. However, it was possible there were other underlying reasons as to why his body took on some of Lamont's physical characteristics.

Chapter 3921 Reinforcements Yan floated over slowly and then gazed at the huge body in a vigilant manner.

There was no doubt about it. This was undoubtedly Zen.

Yan called out.

Rigid, round muscles had swollen to bulges around Zen's face. These special muscles were as tough and indestructible as powerful and refined magical treasures.

His eyes, nose and mouth were almost completely invisible due to those muscles. The sunken structure could now protect his eyes, ears, mouth and nose as much as possible.

However, it was extremely horrible to watch. He looked uglier than a fiend.

Forcing the disgust she was feeling deep inside her, Yan called out once again, "Brother, is that you?"

Zen smiled and reached out his hand to her as if to say 'I am here, sis!' This gesture finally relieved Yan. She took Zen's palm and pouted softly, "Brother, why have you become like this?"

Its bean-sized eyes were full of appraisal for the half-man, half-beast in front of it. "This body may be ugly in your eyes, but it is remarkably strong. It is made for battle!"

Zen had killed a Chaos Ancient God by himself.

He was the first warrior to ever manage that feat in the entire Source World.

Moreover, he had killed Lamont by devouring him, which meant that the killing process had actually made Zen stronger.

This man had really lived up to everyone's expectations.

"Made for battle? Come on. It's too ugly. It doesn't even look human!" Yan said as she sniffed. She wanted the best for her brother.

When it reached about ten feet in height, the shrinking stopped, and Zen's appearance didn't come back either.

As he looked at his fluffy hands and his body the size of a gorilla, his face became a little pale, as if he were afraid.

In the past, whenever he cultivated other strange theurgies, his physical body had also changed, but those changes were controllable, and he had never looked so ugly. If he really couldn't change back, it would be troublesome.

The problem most likely lay in the ancestry-level bloodline.

Just as Zen was about to communicate with the ancestry-level bloodline, a rumble came from the distance.

Looking in the distance, he saw that the noise had been caused by a crack on the ground.

After that, Zen, Yan, King Ieuan and the others saw a giant crack appearing in the distance and spreading towards the edge of the Pear Hill. It didn't stop until it had touched the boundary wall.

After seeing what was happening in the distance, which was crystal clear due to its magnitude, King Ieuan took a deep breath and said, "They have ruined the Taoism Province."

The Taoism Province was the farthest place that could be seen from the Pear Hill. It was normal for dozens of provinces to be ruined when several Chaos Ancient Gods fought. It was impossible to imagine just how much havoc they wreaked everywhere they went.

"I wonder how the Snake Goddess is doing," Yan muttered. She was still worried about the safety of the Snake Goddess and Fuxi.

"Don't worry. They have their real selves with them, so they should be fine," Zen comforted her. He was right.

The strength of the real Fuxi and the real Snake Goddess was high enough to easily fight against a Chaos Ancient God. Coupled with the strength of Eastern Emperor Taiyi, as well as Gerald and Judson on their side, they were surely at a good advantage, if not a great one.

Crack! Crack! Crack! Before anyone could say something, a second crack appeared, and the entire Taoism Province directly disappeared in a pile of dust.

Faced with such a fierce battle, Zen finally couldn't sit still anymore.

If the people of Pear Hill and the Chaos Ancient Gods on their side were really defeated, then they would lose Pear Hill.

The magical ability that the ancestry-level bloodline had just displayed had allowed Zen to devour Lamont. He could feel Lamont struggling inside his body, but as the ancestry-level bloodline continued to change form, it finally managed to digest Lamont and assimilate his powers for Zen's use.

It looked like the ancestry-level bloodline would never let him fall into the hands of the Element Spirit Civilization. This meant that he could easily use the ancestry-level bloodline to his advantage.

"I'll go and have a look. Yan, you protect Pear Hill along with King Ieuan."

Whoosh! Zen floated in the air and disappeared, leaving a burst of shadows behind him like a rocket trail.

Two huge cracks had appeared right in the heart of the Taoism Province, like the two jaws of a monster trying to devour the province.

Giant brown chaotic clouds were floating quietly under those cracks.

Suddenly, they began to surge, and a golden sword light rushed out, which stirred the heaven and earth.

Splash! Splash! Splash! The sword light extended around for tens of millions of feet and stabbed towards one side of the chaotic clouds.

Bang! Bang! Bang! It seemed like the golden sword light collided with something solid inside those clouds, and the crisp sound it caused could be heard across tens of millions of miles. Any creature that was too close to the clouds would have been shattered by the intense sound wave! Whoosh! However, unable to break that solid object with several consecutive strikes, the attacker rapidly retreated.

After something rushed out of the chaotic clouds, everyone finally saw who the attacker was. He was Eastern Emperor Taiyi, and he had activated the Wild God Body and was now more than six million feet in height! "Oh you want to escape? It's too late for that!"

Just as Eastern Emperor Taiyi was about to retreat, he bumped into an invisible wall. With a groan, he rolled over and tried to cross the wall from the other side. However, both sides of the wall were sealed by an invisible force field, and he was trapped! The next moment, Othniel appeared outside the wall. His single eye, gigantic in size, was filled with a trace of anger and depression.

The strength that the Pear Hill had displayed in this fight was far beyond his expectations. Eastern Emperor Taiyi, Fuxi and the Snake Goddess had already made several powerful strikes. Gerald and Judson were also on the opponents' team.

If it weren't for the Grandmaster of Heaven, Othniel and Herbert would have already been defeated and the battle would have been over.

While the Grandmaster of Heaven was busy fighting Gerald and Judson, Othniel had managed to find a chance to trap Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

However, Eastern Emperor Taiyi didn't seem too worried by the fact that he had been trapped.

Buzz! A strong bloodline power darted out of his body, and a golden sword light surged, spreading across the entire visible space.

Bang! Bang! Bang! The sword light bounced back and forth, like laser beams between mirrors in the space that had trapped Eastern Emperor Taiyi. However, the space seemed remarkably stable. It could not be destroyed so easily.

"It's useless to struggle. Our bloodlines determine the difference in our strength," Othniel sneered.

With a flash of blue light that rushed out of his eye, several smaller spaces began to appear in a crisscross fashion across the space that had trapped Eastern Emperor Taiyi. Othniel seemed to want to use these small spaces to directly cut Eastern Emperor Taiyi into countless pieces.

When the small spaces began to appear, they immediately targeted Eastern Emperor Taiyi's body and locked on to him. Numerous large and small cuts appeared on the surface of his body. The cuts continued to deepen rapidly, and blood began to flow out.

Just as Othniel was about to breathe a sigh of relief with the feeling that he had finally defeated at least one of the opponents, a small figure suddenly appeared at the top of the spaces he had created.

Chapter 3922 Struggle Zen's appearance hadn't returned to normal; he was still a ten feet tall monster and in this form, his aura had also undergone a huge change.

At a glance, Othniel could not recognize him. But under current circumstances, any creature daring to come down could not be ordinary.

Swoosh...

The blue light in Othniel's only eye flickered and a space formed on either side of Zen.

If these spaces could restrain him, he'd be able to cut him in half with ease.

But as soon as they enveloped Zen's body, they dissipated immediately! "What?"

Othniel was dumbfounded and he quickly thought of Zen in his mind. Was this monster actually him? This thought lingered in his mind when Zen suddenly grew even more, to a monster more than eight million feet tall! When Zen had previously activated his Wild God Body, he was only capable of expanding to around four million feet high. Before he had activated it this time, he still believed that was his limit.

He now realized, however, that his body had doubled in size! Was it because he had devoured Lamont? Othniel had a bad feeling about this.

Zen had been able to break the Grandmaster of Heaven's Fishing Drum, and the triangular world he had summoned, quite easily. If this horrific monster truly was Zen, he was now stuck in quite a terrible situation.

Even more curious were Lamont's features that this monster shared; such as his long, strong arms with the white hair on them.

"Who are you?" Othniel asked brazenly, raising his head.

All Zen offered was an ugly smile. He then raised his foot and stamped down lightly, creating a huge crater in the space that imprisoned the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi! "It really is him..."

Othniel was now sure it was Zen; only he could break through his space barrier so quickly and easily.

But why had he become this monstrosity...

He was still lost in confusion when the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi had thrust his sword out, sending countless golden rays of sword radiance bursting out.

Phew! The space already had a big hole in it and now the sword radiance obliterated it into pieces.

"Swish, swish, swish..."

The sharp golden radiance covered Othniel like a net.

His space barrier could hold the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi, but it didn't mean he had the power to do as he pleased to him.

Once the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi had pushed his own bloodline to the limit, he displayed an outrageous and terrifying level of swordsmanship. If Othniel wasn't careful, he'd be sliced up for sure.

He retreated as fast as he could, at the same time clapping his hands and creating space shields ten million feet wide, one after the other.

Bang! Bang! Bang...

The real Eastern Emperor Taiyi chased him down relentlessly, shattering every space shield he came across.

The golden sword light was like the God of Death, not resting until it had taken him! He then went all out, doing all he could to shake off the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi. As he did, he suddenly felt a space fluctuation from above.

As the Chaos Ancient God in charge of the space truth, Othniel was extremely sensitive to space fluctuations, and as soon as he felt it, he knew it was Zen who had begun attacking him! "Buzz..."

He pointed upwards as a reflex and a space fluctuation surrounded Zen, ready to exile him to a corner of the chaos.

Othniel had lost sight of the fact that his original intention of attacking the Pear Hill was to complete the Element Spirit race's mission - capture Zen at all costs.

But he now planned to exile him because he felt threatened! It mattered not. As the space fluctuations gathered on Zen's body, they disappeared instantly, without a trace...

It was then that Othniel felt clearly that Zen's body had given off a space fluctuation opposite to his to counter his exile force! "How is this possible?"

Othniel's eye was overflowed with disbelief.

A power absolutely opposite to his own power of space actually existed in the chaos? If he hadn't seen it with his own eye, he wouldn't have believed it. More to it, Zen had pulled it off so effortlessly.

Othniel still hung in a state of astonishment when Zen pounced over and seized him from behind into his tight grip.

"Swish, swish, swish..."

From not far off, the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi took this opportunity to attack, the golden sword radiance exploding and inflicting many bloody holes on Othniel's body.

Othniel then desperately activated his bloodline power to teleport himself away. The blue space truth circled around his body, making him seem like an object about to disappear. His body morphed back and forth between a shadow and a real body of substance, popping in and out of view.

Puff! Puff! Puff! Puff! Puff! Othniel continued struggling as sixteen ribs as sharp as swords, shot out of Zen's chest and pierced into his body. Then the barbs that grew from the ribs bound the two bodies firmly together.

The real Eastern Emperor Taiyi had been in Zen's inner world this whole time, so he had a general understanding of the ancestry-level bloodline within him. Even so, what he saw now shocked him to his core. How did this kid have such an attack method? Othniel felt the pain and knew something bad was about to happen.

There was still a considerable gap between him and Lamont in their abilities to use truth-level theurgies.

Lamont was skilled at controlling temperature. Relying on extreme cold, he was almost immune to all energy attacks. This was why the Divine Crystal Array of King Leuan had failed to hurt him.

As for Othniel, his skill lay in controlling space and his theurgy was unparalleled in confinement and escape! With a roar, Othniel's body suddenly collapsed like a tower made of sand. Every grain of sand within his body turned into a Minimum Space, which was the smallest matter in the chaos. Only then did Othniel finally rid himself of Zen's control.

An eight-foot tall person was made up of tens of billions of Minimum Spaces. Othniel's massive body possessed way more than that.

Innumerable Minimum Spaces, indistinguishable to the naked eye, moved to another spot where Othniel's body gradually reformed. This process was, however, heavily draining for him.

When he finally looked at Zen again, fear filled his eye as he realized that if he had not just put everything he had into escaping, he would probably have lost his life. What Zen said next proved him right.

"Impressive. Your method is much smarter than Lamont's, but that's it." The voice that rang from his chest sounded very strange.

Othniel suddenly widened his eye. "Lamont has descended to the Pear Hill? What happened to him?"

In his heart he already knew the answer. The white hair and the pair of arms on Zen's body told him all he needed to know but it was still hard to accept that a Chaos Ancient God had died at Zen's hands.

After all, for as long as one could recall, a human had never killed a Chaos Ancient God.

As existences that controlled the truth in the chaos, the Chaos Ancient Gods were thought to be invincible.

"He is dead," Zen said decisively, giving Othniel the answer he least wanted to hear.

Chapter 3923 Lawless Cage It was true that there were many forces in the chaos, but it didn't make things complicated.

After the six Chaos Ancient Gods split into two factions, the division of powers in the Source World became quite stable.

Fuxi was the one who wanted to complete the Finale Way the most. He tried his best to make himself stronger, enough to kill the Chaos Ancient Gods and break the balance.

The only thing was that the Chaos Ancient Gods were invincible, and this was one of the truths in the chaos.

He couldn't break that truth, but Zen had surprisingly done it.

Othniel looked at Zen again, but this time with a hint of fear and caution.

After all, the Chaos Ancient Gods were not immortal. Anyone whose life was on the line, like him, would be on guard.

Although he already believed what Zen said, he still countered, "Just you? Don't brag about yourself!"

Zen glanced at him indifferently and said, "You'll know whether I'm bragging or not soon."

As he spoke, he suddenly disappeared from where he stood.

Moreover, his disappearance didn't cause any space fluctuation, nor did he build a space channel.

It was as if he had used another theurgy that never existed before to teleport! Naturally, Othniel was shocked when he saw that Zen had disappeared.

After all, he was a Chaos Ancient God in charge of the space truth. What skillful method did Zen use to avoid his detection? "Buzz!"

His eye glowed a bright blue then he released a mighty truth power. That was when he finally noticed something.

There was an immensely thin line in the black void that moved like a worm as it swiftly approached him.

When he got to see it more clearly, it was already quite close to him! "Go!"

In turn, he used the Grand Teleportation without a second thought.

Zen had already jumped out from the end of the line the moment Othniel disappeared, but it was too late. Othniel had already teleported far away.

"He actually spotted me. If it was any other Chaos Ancient God, they probably couldn't have done that." Zen shrugged.

After the ancestry-level bloodline devoured Lamont, it naturally became more interested in consuming Chaos Ancient Gods.

The ancestry-level bloodline also played an active role when Zen dealt with Othniel. For instance, the bloodline released this particular space theurgy that even Othniel found it hard to see through it. Zen almost succeeded in devouring him just now.

Even though Othniel could also still turn into multiple Minimum Spaces to escape, such a method consumed a lot of energy, and he might not be able to get away after a few uses.

As for Zen, he failed to catch Othniel at his first attempt. At that point, he turned around and nodded at the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

The real Eastern Emperor Taiyi understood what Zen meant. His eyes flashed with a sharp light, and the long sword in his hand turned into golden lights that filled the sky and swept towards Othniel. At the same time, Zen disappeared again.

Othniel dodged the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi's golden sword radiance and simultaneously watched out for the curved line.

The line was easy to miss, and it was almost impossible to distinguish it among the bright golden sword radiance.

But the moment he stopped, the line appeared behind him out of nowhere.

Meanwhile, Zen's ribs extended and seized him from behind once again! "Puff, puff, puff, puff..."

The thick, sharp ribs pierced through his body and left sixteen gaping, bloody holes on it.

This time, he did not struggle anymore. He immediately turned into trillions of Minimum Spaces and escaped from Zen's arms before his body condensed and took shape again.

However, although he was powerful, he felt exhausted the second time he turned into multiple Minimum Spaces.

Just as he took shape again, Zen disappeared and turned into a thin line once more, then flew straight towards him. He didn't even have a chance to catch his breath! As he observed Zen's aggressive attack, he only sighed and finally chose to exile.

He couldn't exile Zen, but he could exile himself.

When Zen appeared at the end of the thin line, Othniel had already gone to the edge of the Source World.

"He didn't use the Grand Teleportation this time?" Of course, he was surprised.

"He must have exiled himself. I'm afraid it will take some time to get him back," the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi said with certainty.

"He sure ran fast," Zen muttered with a shrug. At that point, the chaos cloud in the distance burst and unleashed a strong energy fluctuation.

He and the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi glanced at each other, then swiftly went straight for the chaos cloud.

The chaos cloud was incomparably enormous. It was so big that a body millions of feet high was only like a drop in the ocean compared to it! Outside the chaos cloud were sixteen tall purple pillars that floated in the air. Each purple pillar was painted with mysterious patterns and contained vast amounts of hidden power.

Then, the purple pillars turned into a perfect cage and trapped all those from the Pear Hill inside it.

The real Fuxi, the real Snake Goddess, Gerald, and Judson all had suffered heavy injuries.

There was a big hole one million feet wide on the real Fuxi's chest. A black fire burned on the hole to prevent the horrible wound from healing.

On the other hand, Judson lost an arm, and half of his head got broken.

However, Gerald looked the worst of them all. Both of his pincers were damaged.

Only the real Snake Goddess looked slightly better. Although she was not injured, her face still looked fatigued. The battle with the Grandmaster of Heaven had cost a lot of her energy.

Gerald's life truth-level theurgy could immediately heal all their wounds, but the black fire kept their wounds burning at bay.

The black fire was the nemesis of the life truth. Back then, it took Gerald a lot of time to get rid of the black fire when it burned him once. Now that he was currently in an intense battle, he didn't have time to help his companions deal with the fire.

Furthermore, the cage formed by the purple pillars was the Lawless Cage, which Herbert had made using the confinement truth.

Therefore, the warriors who were inside it lost half their strength.

The Grandmaster of Heaven stood on one of the purple pillars and looked down at them. "I can give you a chance to join our Nihility race and surrender to me," he said with a cold smile.

As Herbert, who had built the Lawless Cage, heard those words, his face instantly darkened.

It was true that the Grandmaster of Heaven was powerful, but Herbert also contributed greatly in subduing the four warriors.

Also, his stand was completely different from the Grandmaster of Heaven's.

The only reason they worked together was that they wanted to fight against the Pear Hill. After that, a battle would probably ensue between them.

Now, the Grandmaster of Heaven wanted to make all the people of the Pear Hill surrender to him. How could he accept that? "Grandmaster of Heaven, you and I worked together in order to take down the Pear Hill. These people can't be restrained; they can only be killed," he said bluntly.

The Grandmaster of Heaven turned to look at him and sneered, "Why should I listen to you?"

"I also did my part to take them down," he threatened. "If I remove the Lawless Cage, I'm afraid you'll also be in trouble."

No matter how strong the Grandmaster of Heaven was, it was hard for him to deal with the two Chaos Ancient Gods at the same time. What was more, the real Fuxi and the real Snake Goddess were there as well, so he was less likely to win the fight.

"This Lawless Cage is indeed powerful, but I'm afraid you are not the only one who could control it," the Grandmaster of Heaven said nonchalantly and ignored the threat. Suddenly, four of the sixteen purple pillars rose and trapped Herbert.

Chapter 3924 The Desperate End Back then, the Grandmaster of Heaven had made a contract with Othniel using the Contract-restricting Twin-headed Snake.

According to the contract, he would not attack Othniel before taking down Pear Hill.

However, the contract didn't mention anything about Herbert.

Now that he had taken advantage of Herbert to capture the people of Pear Hill and possessed the same abilities as the latter, Herbert no longer had any value to him. "What do you mean by doing so, Grandmaster of Heaven?"

Herbert's face darkened.

He already felt that he had gotten quite weaker in the Lawless Cage.

If he completely lost control of the Lawless Cage, then the Grandmaster of Heaven could do anything to him.

"I'm eliminating my future enemies in advance. Is there anything wrong about that?" the Grandmaster of Heaven stated matter-of-factly.

As the head of the Nihility race, the Grandmaster of Heaven was one of the Element Spirit Civilization's mortal enemies. It was inevitable for him to confront Herbert.

"You..."

Herbert's body began to glow brightly as he tried hard to activate his bloodline power.

As the powerful energy surged in his body, the purple pillars also began to glow. It was clear that he was scrambling for control over the Lawless Cage.

If he was still outside the Lawless Cage, he could've probably defeated the Grandmaster of Heaven with his excellent understanding of the truth power.

But now, the Lawless Cage greatly limited his strength. His struggle only lasted for a few seconds before victory was declared.

In the end, he had to admit defeat to the Grandmaster of Heaven. "As the leader of the Nihility race, you are shameful to be such a treacherous man!"

Herbert snapped resentfully.

"I never swore anything to you. What made me treacherous?" the Grandmaster of Heaven said with a shrug.

"You..." At that point, Herbert was too angry to speak anymore.

Unlike the other Chaos Ancient Gods, he rarely traveled around the mortal world. Thus, he didn't know about such lies and deceit.

"Hmph, the Nihility race and the Element Spirit Civilization are all the same. They only come to you when they need something from you, then they will kill you the moment you're of no use to them. I tried to convince you before, but you ignored my words like nothing!" Fuxi suddenly shouted from the side.

Fuxi had lent his body to the real Fuxi, but he still got detained in the end.

Still, he didn't blame it on the real Fuxi.

After all, things might have ended up worse if he had personally fought in the battle.

When he saw that Herbert also got incarcerated in the Lawless Cage, he couldn't help but grab control of his body again so he could sneer at Herbert.

In the past, he had almost won Herbert over to their side. However, the latter finally believed other people's lies and chose to follow the Purge Way.

As for Herbert, he was enraged at first, but expressed mockery upon hearing Fuxi's words. "Isn't Pear Hill the leader of the Finale Way? You thought you were right and justified, but all of you just ended up like me!"

he retorted.

At that moment, Fuxi, the real Snake Goddess, Gerald, and Judson, all felt downhearted.

The end of chaos would bring about destruction sooner or later.

The chaos had already experienced many ends now. When the ends of the previous rounds of chaos came, people still had a chance to fight back. In this round, however, they didn't even get to try. It was truly pathetic.

"Even if we can't complete the Finale Way in this round of chaos, we will have another chance in the next round," Fuxi shot back.

Herbert laughed and pointed towards the Grandmaster of Heaven. "Now that victory belongs to him and the Nihility race, do you think there will be another round of chaos?" he scoffed.

Fuxi glanced at the Grandmaster of Heaven, and he finally felt hopeless.

He and the Snake Goddess knew their mission very well ever since the establishment of Pear Hill. The Finale Way remained engraved in their bones, and they were not afraid to sacrifice themselves for it.

He believed that after many rounds of chaos, a noble hero would emerge and lead them to their victory.

If they could not do it after trying one thousand times, then they would try ten thousand times. If they could not do it after trying ten thousand times, then one hundred thousand times.

Besides, time was quite cheap compared to their eternal cause. As long as it was still possible to complete the Finale Way, they would eventually succeed after countless attempts. That was Fuxi's belief.

However, at that moment, he realized that he had underestimated the Nihility race. They were simply a group of insane monsters! The most incredible thing about it all was that the leader of the Nihility race was a real human! "Youâ€¦ Why did you choose the Nihility Way?" Fuxi raised his head and asked.

The connection between the Grandmaster of Heaven and the 77th civilization was clear to the real Fuxi and the real Snake Goddess, but not to him.

"You are just a replica. It's meaningless for you to know much," the Grandmaster of Heaven said indifferently. "You just need to know that if you want to live, you have to submit to me!" he declared.

As soon as he finished speaking, he shook his long sleeve then a black ship came out of it.

The captain of the Black Ship leaped out from the bow and simultaneously activated the Wild God Body. Then, he summoned the Contract-restricting Twin-headed Snake.

"Make your vow before the Contract-restricting Twin-headed Snake. If you submit to the Grandmaster of Heaven and join the Nihility race, you can live," said the captain.

Generally speaking, not even a Chaos Ancient God could escape the restrictions of such contracts. Once they took an oath, they had to follow it all their lives.

"If you refuse, I'll send you to hell," the Grandmaster of Heaven stated in a deathly calm voice as if he didn't care about their choices at all.

Fuxi, the real Snake Goddess, Judson, Gerald and Herbert all fell silent.

Warriors at their level could afford to accept death, but they still had to consider their companions' situations if they died.

Most importantly, defeat in this war would probably cost Pear Hill everything.

"My time is limited," the Grandmaster of Heaven chirped as he gently brandished the Cyan Misty Sword. Cyan sword radiance mixed with black fire swayed on the edge of the weapon.

This battle only eliminated Pear Hill's forces, and the Grandmaster of Heaven knew he hadn't won the final victory yet. Next, he had to deal with the Element Spirit Civilization. The battle against them might take place in the chaos or the Other Shore.

Since no one had spoken yet, he shot the cyan sword radiance at them.

Puff! Puff! Puff! Puff! The strike punctured all of their chests, and black flames burned hotly in their wounds.

Although such injuries weren't enough to kill them, the black fire still felt like torture. Everyone's faces twisted in pain.

However, even though the black fire burned continuously, all of them in the Lawless Cage endured it silently without yielding.

"I only want to recruit more men in the chaos who could be of use to me, but it looks like you are all strong-willed people. Since you refuse to join me, let me send you to hell."

With a murderous glint, the Grandmaster of Heaven waved his hand, and the entire Lawless Cage began to shrink rapidly.

The distance between the purple pillars continued to lessen, while the pressure inside the cage increased.

Fuxi, the Snake Goddess, and the others still tried hard to resist the black fire, but they had quite a hard time now that the Lawless Cage was also shrinking.

As they became increasingly powerless to resist, the black fire burned more and more wildly on their bodies and brought death closer to them.

Buzz! Just then, a golden sword radiance crossed a vast distance and slashed squarely on the Lawless Cage.

The mighty golden sword radiance was powerful enough to go against the Grandmaster of Heaven's cyan sword radiance. Its attack rocked the entire Lawless Cage quite violently, which weakened the cage's restraints.

Therefore, the Snake Goddess and the others inside it had a chance to breathe.

"Eastern Emperor Taiyi?"

The Grandmaster of Heaven raised his head and looked at the figure in the far end of the horizon. He had thought that it would be Othniel who came out of the battleground victoriously, but that was not the case.

Chapter 3925 Unexpected Appearance The real Eastern Emperor Taiyi was not weak by any means, but he was no match for Othniel.

That was why it shocked the Grandmaster of Heaven a great deal to see him walking towards them.

Fuxi, the real Snake Goddess, Gerald and Judson also sported expressions of surprise on their faces, while Herbert even bordered on desperation.

In a flash, the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi spiraled into the air and brandished his golden sword radiance.

Buzz! Buzz! Buzz! Buzz...

His bloodline-activated swordsmanship was geared to the max as nineteen golden long swords were summoned by his side.

These golden swords looked illusory and extended far into the distance.

Some directly stabbed into the Source World, but did not really damage it.

A few sensitive creatures felt their hearts palpitate but nothing more.

The blades, however, were very solid and even the toughest magic treasure in the chaos could be slashed open by them easily.

Buzz! With a shrill, ear-shattering whistle, the nineteen golden swords merged into one and immediately slashed down towards the Grandmaster of Heaven.

At the moment before impact, the light emanated from the blade and formed a golden arc in the air. A terrifying force was released from the sword as the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi was going to break through the Lawless Cage and pierce through the Grandmaster of Heaven.

Fuxi's eyes sparkled in excitement. "Eastern Emperor Taiyi is so powerful!"

In contrast, the real Snake Goddess was calm and the real Fuxi sighed slightly.

The real Eastern Emperor Taiyi was by no means weak, but the gap between him and the Grandmaster of Heaven was way too big. Even if he pushed that physical body to the limit, his efforts would remain futile.

They had no idea how the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi defeated Othniel, but it would be impossible for him to change the situation now.

In the face of such a seemingly devastating attack, the Grandmaster of Heaven only snorted as he lifted his own Cyan Misty Sword to resist his oncoming opponent's attack.

His sword was fixed and stayed motionless atop his head.

Bang! Upon the moment of impact with the Cyan Misty Sword, the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi's golden sword trembled. However, the Cyan Misty Sword remained motionless.

With eyes full of determination, the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi clenched his hand and lifted his sword to let out a series of slashes upon his opponent.

Bang! Bang! Bang! This golden sword was his strongest theurgy, but it remained unable to shake the Cyan Misty Sword that kept resisting each attack.

During the course of the one-sided struggle, the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi tried to change the direction of his strikes in an attempt to kill his target but to no avail.

All the Grandmaster of Heaven did was flicking his finger and blocking each of his pursuer's sword strikes.

After ten strikes, the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi's sword showed signs of fatigue and the golden light was significantly dimmer than before.

"I have no idea how you managed to escape Othniel, but since you're brave enough to come at me and court death, then I will fulfill your wish," the Grandmaster of Heaven muttered darkly as he went through the purple pillars and headed straight towards the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi! As soon as he got out of the Lawless Cage, Herbert immediately tried to gain control. However, the Grandmaster of Heaven merely turned around and silenced him with a glare. Soon enough, several purple pillars flashed and suppressed Herbert.

Meanwhile, the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi remained resolute and had no plans to retreat. He continued to wave his dimmed golden sword and hacked away at the Grandmaster of Heaven.

Whoosh! It was a battle of blades as each strike from the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi was deflected by the Grandmaster of Heaven's Cyan Misty Sword. In the blink of an eye, the latter appeared in front of his opponent, slashing at him with his Cyan Misty Sword in order to conclude this fight.

"Go to hell!" the Grandmaster of Heaven shouted.

However, in the split second that he was about to deal his blow, the Grandmaster of Heaven saw a look of ridicule on the real Eastern Emperor Taiyi's face with no trace of cowardice whatsoever.

How could someone make such an expression in the face of death? Momentarily distracted by his confusion, the Grandmaster of Heaven was caught off-guard when he felt a piercing sensation at the back of his neck that soon escalated into indescribable pain.

He turned around on reflex and saw a huge, ugly, gorilla-like monster in front of him.

"Fuck off!" he screamed just as the monster was about to hug him.

His reaction was extremely fast and he was able to predict what would happen next.

Puff, puff, puff...

Chapter 3926 Breaking The Lawless Cage Even before the battle began, Zen's body had already started mutating, and the Snake Goddess had noticed it.

Chapter 3927 The Foundation The Grandmaster of Heaven had worked hard to come up with the situation.

Chapter 3928 The Origin Of The Light Region Raising his Cyan Misty Sword high, the Grandmaster of Heaven had a white light column strike him.

Chapter 3929 Join Hands Theoretically, the four quadrants of the ancestry-level bloodline contained all the abilities.

What seemed like an ordinary palm strike vibrated for over ten thousand times as it came into contact with the chest of the Grandmaster of Heaven.

Fuxi's goal was not to kill the Grandmaster of Heaven but to weaken his defense of his Sanskrit Light Body as much as possible.

Next, Gerald appeared. He waved his tail and stabbed right at the center of the Grandmaster of Heaven's chest, exactly where Fuxi's palm hit.

Gerald's strikes were so powerful that even Claire had been killed in his hands by the Poison of Decomposition. If the Grandmaster of Heaven was pierced deeply enough, he would die the same way Claire did.

Chapter 3930 Press More than half of Gerald's bright-colored tail needle was impaled into the Sanskrit Light Body of the Grandmaster of Heaven.

The tail needle was about three hundred thousand feet long, and about twothirds of the total length was drilled deep into the body.

Ideally, it was already enough to break the Sanskrit Light Body.

"Nice work, Gerald!"

"There's no way he could resist the Poison of Decomposition!"

"Finish him!"

Everyone yelled and was full of expectations.

Technically, the Poison of Decomposition was not a poison, but a kind of energy that could destroy things at a molecular level. Supposedly, no one had a good way to withstand it.

Just when everyone thought that they had finally succeeded, the expression on Gerald's face gradually changed. "What is this? There is noâ€”"

"Physical body?" the Grandmaster of Heaven sneered as he finished Gerald's sentence.

Everyone clearly witnessed how Gerald's needle pierced into the Sanskrit Light Body of the Grandmaster of Heaven. However, the body was empty.

It turned out that it was not a real physical body.

"So what? That doesn't matter!" Gerald retorted, trying to still sound confident.

The Poison of Decomposition was supposed to destroy everything, including energies and souls. That was why Gerald was still confident that they could take the Grandmaster of Heaven down.

Soon, a black mass leaked at the place where the needle stabbed the body.

Like a thick dripping ink, it began to diffuse but soon stopped.

In just a matter of seconds, the all-conquering Poison of Decomposition was subdued and lost its effect.

"Are you done with your childish games?!"

the Grandmaster of Heaven shouted contemptuously.

Then, at his bidding, his long sword emerged, shrouded in pure bright lights.

He waved his sword and a white sword arc instantly appeared in the void.

The sword arc was lashing in the air at such an incredible speed.

Upon seeing this, Gerald quickly pulled his tail and retrieved it from the body of the Grandmaster of Heaven. However, there was not enough time.

Splat! Gerald's tail was slashed, and a stream of green blood gushed out immediately.

The Grandmaster of Heaven raised his sword and aimed at Gerald again.

The sharp lights coming from it seemed to be able to illuminate the entire chaos.

This time, as the Grandmaster of Heaven threw his second strike, Gerald's reaction was quicker. He was able to use the Grand Teleportation in order to avoid the incoming attack.

"Humph! What an annoying insect!"

The Grandmaster of Heaven was going all out. He intended to do anything and release everything in his arsenal just to bring down all his opponents.

With that, he prepared his next set of attacks.

Suddenly, the space around him solidified. He dragged the white shadows of light and instantly appeared in front of Fuxi.

"So fast! I won't make it!"

His body froze for a few seconds before it could react.

Compared to the Grandmaster of Heaven's lightning speed, everyone else seemed to move so slow.

The Grandmaster of Heaven admitted that these Chaos Ancient Gods and Eternal Realm masters were formidable. Even if he was omnipotent, he was still hindered by their tenacious skills and methods.

Herbert, who was now on the side of the Pear Hill, activated his other theurgy. In a flash, six lightning-like columns began to take shape around the Grandmaster of Heaven.

He was so busy activating his bloodline power to set up the Slaughter Prison that he didn't notice the light. Suddenly, the light expanded, and that was the only time that Herbert noted it.

However, it was too late when Herbert noticed it.

The white light instantly formed a sturdy space that trapped Herbert within.

Herbert realized that his life was in great danger. He did all he could in order to break the light column.

However, the light column was so indestructible that even the ancestry-level bloodline was not able to destroy it. Previously, it had to produce tentacles to absorb the column bit by bit. So Herbert, who only used brute force to break it, didn't make it budge even a little.

Crash! Suddenly, an unusual noise resounded from within the light column.

Herbert's movements were stopped as if there was an extremely powerful force that was pressing on his body.

The downward pressure in the light column continued to grow stronger and stronger, crushing Herbert's body little by little.

After a short while, Herbert's body was tightly pressed at the bottom of the light column.

Crash! Crack! Herbert's bones began to break and his body was starting to collapse.

Splat! Hebert's entire body exploded and was completely crushed.

His huge body, which was millions of feet tall, was reduced into a puddle of blood. Everyone couldn't believe that a dignified Chaos Ancient God could die in this miserable way.

Gerald, Judson, Fuxi, and the Snake Goddess didn't avert their eyes from the scene. Instead, their faces darkened and their eyes were filled with rage.

At this time, the Grandmaster of Heaven had finally removed all the golden vines that were wrapped on his body. There was a smirk on his face, yet an extreme murderous intent was oozing from his eyes.

He was getting impatient because his real enemy wasn't there. Originally, he did not intend to use too much of his foundation power, but these people gave him a hard time. With that, he decided to handle them using a fiercer method.

"Are you mad? Well, you ask for it! Now, I'll kill you one by one!"

Gerald became instantly aware when the Grandmaster of Heaven pointed at his direction. He knew immediately that something bad was about to happen. He quickly tried to flee, but the light column was already forming before he could even move from his position.

Then, the pressure inside the light column suddenly increased. Instantly, Gerald's body was pressed at the bottom.

Chapter 3931 Pressing Forward The miserable death which Herbert had suffered was still lingering on everyone's mind. Trapped and unable to escape, Gerald was obviously about to end up the same.

Although they knew that the light column was almost completely invulnerable, they still had to try. Therefore, they launched their attacks in unison, trying to destroy the light column that had trapped Gerald.

Even under their attacks, the pressure in the light column increased sharply, and the hard shell on the surface of Gerald's body began to emit cracking sounds. Countless cracks spread out, like lines of minuscule bugs crawling over his body.

Gerald himself also knew how powerful the light column was. Trapped inside, he had to try and make an effort to save himself since no one else could do so.

Buzz! A green colored light began to leak out from the cracks.

The Grandmaster of Heaven felt the strong life energy that was contained within the light column with a look of contempt on his face.

Gerald was a Chaos Ancient God who had mastered the truth of life.

However, it was impossible for him to use that power to repair his body.

"Huh! Don't try to struggle. It is useless,"

the Grandmaster of Heaven sneered. And as soon as his words finished, the squeezing force in the light column doubled suddenly.

Crack! Crack! Crack! With a wispy, cracking sound, Gerald's shell was suddenly broken completely. Under the irresistible pressure, the tissues in his body began to bleed profusely, and his huge and fragile compound eyes exploded outside.

However, the truth power surrounding him did not try to repair his body. It could not. Instead, it was transforming his body.

The truth was, even if it did try, it was useless to repair the broken shell.

The shell was just a broken defense mechanism. It was not suitable for such a high pressure environment.

The truth power was instead growing a thin layer of tissue over the hard shell. The tissue was flat and weirdly thin, as if it were made of countless pieces of paper.

This was the only visible change on the surface of Gerald's body. At the same time, several more changes were taking place inside him.

The squeezed body tissue was quickly being transformed by the truth power. Gerald's height was being reduced constantly. Finally, he became completely flat. In fact, that was what he wanted to do.

In a short while, the originally scorpion shaped Gerald had turned into a thin pie.

This was a highly powerful move. Some fishes in the deep sea had to bear intense sea water pressure all year round, which had evolved their bodies into flat shapes. However, they needed millions of years to evolve, but Gerald had done this in an instant.

A green light flickered on the side of his flat body, and a pair of slender eyes grew to observe everything around him.

"What the hell?"

The Grandmaster of Heaven was confused now.

Herbert had also been crushed into a meat pie just now, and therefore the Grandmaster of Heaven hadn't paid much attention to the change in Gerald's body. But the strong life energy that had leaked out could not repair Gerald's body, which had surprised him a bit.

Maybe the repair speed was not as fast as the squeezing speed. Therefore, he had not thought much about it. And yet, after a few seconds, Gerald still had a lot of life energy left and there wasn't much damage to him.

When the Grandmaster of Heaven realized what had happened, he sneered, "Your desire to survive is strong. In this form, your pressure bearing ability has increased by at least six times. But that is still in vain!"

Once he had finished speaking, his palm emitted a strong white light.

From the way he was utilizing his strength, the power of the foundation seemed to be inexhaustible. The squeezing force in the light column continued to increase even now.

Now, Zen no longer resembled a human from any angle. Instead, he looked like an octopus.

The Grandmaster of Heaven looked at the octopus-like Zen with a cold expression in his eyes.

Previously, it had taken Zen a long time to break the light column, but now, he was powerful enough to easily break the column. This was after he had disappeared for just a little while.

Such a speed of growth in strength was unimaginable. Zen was omnipotent now! An opponent with power of this magnitude was going to be extremely tricky to deal with.

As he retreated rapidly, a blue light flashed in his eyes. Once he had located Zen, he reached out his hand and grabbed at something in the air. With a buzzing sound, a light column materialized and covered Zen.

As Zen's tentacles absorbed the wall of the light column for a while, the wall was broken down once again. The light column was able to hinder Zen for just a single second.

Splash! Splash! Splash! All the light columns were broken by Zen.

If one observed carefully, the suckers on his tentacles were subtly changing shape during the whole process.

In the beginning, the suckers had been circular, but now they had slowly evolved into a diamond-shaped structure. That way, they could absorb the Great Sanskrit Light much more efficiently. The speed at which they could break the light columns was increasing with every strike, which left the Grandmaster of Heaven flabbergasted.

Gerald, who was quickly repairing his body, along with Judson, Fuxi, and the Snake Goddess quietly watched the scene unfold before their eyes, without any intention of interfering. They knew their presence wouldn't make much of a difference in this battle.

What confused the Grandmaster of Heaven was that after breaking the light columns, Zen could have just moved forward to attack him. If he were caught by Zen's tentacles, he would definitely die.

However, Zen was pressing forward very slowly. What was he up to? While the Grandmaster of Heaven was lost in thought and trying to understand what was going on, a thin line was floating in the void behind him.

When he finally approached the thin line unwittingly, a mass of tentacles appeared out of nowhere and swallowed him.

Chapter 3932 My Will These particular tentacles came from the one that had been cut off by the Grandmaster of Heaven.

The ancestry-level bloodline refused to be divided, and even the ones that were divided were very eager to return.

However, just this one time, the ancestry-level bloodline allowed this individual to stay apart, hide in space, and continue to reproduce on its own.

The suckers of the tentacles aggressively absorbed the Great Sanskrit Light while he was desperately struggling.

The voice of the Grandmaster of Heaven became softer and softer until it was inaudible. Soon after, his entire body completely vanished.

After the Grandmaster of Heaven activated his Sanskrit Light Body, not one member of the Black Ship joined the fray.

"Zen could actually destroy the Grandmaster of Heaven's Sanskrit Light Body. His strength cannot be underestimated anymore,"

the captain uttered to himself.

Not long ago, the captain had only treated Zen as his junior.

But in just a short time, Zen was able to surpass and even kill the person that he looked up to.

The Grandmaster of Heaven was the leader of the Nihility race.

Furthermore, he was known for his outstanding strength on the Other Shore.

"What are you talking about? That's not even his own power," Shera said, shaking her head as if unwilling to accept the fact that the Grandmaster of Heaven fell in the hands of Zen.

The Evil God instantly flew and crashed on the deck of the Black Ship. A huge hole was created where he landed.

The Evil God slowly crawled out of the hole, still wearing a smug look on his face. "What? Did I say something wrong? Ha-ha! Why would you even defend the reputation of someone who failed because of his weakness?" He wasn't apologetic at all.

As the brass man heard his impious laughter, his rage started contorting his face.
