Meanwhile, three white balls floated on one side of the ice piece.

Hot flames burned steadily in the center of one of the white balls. Not long after, a young girl's head appeared. It was none other than Claire.

The moment Claire took shape, thunder and lightning cracked inside the white ball beside her and outlined a burly human figure. It turned out to be Les, the second of the three backbones of the Element Spirit Civilization.

"A human boy actually defeated the Grandmaster of Heaven! Ha-ha-ha!"

Les laughed in a hoarse voice.

"My instincts never fail me," Claire said seriously, "though it's a pity that such a talent can't work for us."

"So, he could only dieâ€¦"

This delicate voice came from the last white ball, which contained a strange-looking life form.

The creature looked like a cold armor but had a pair of long light wings on the back.

He was the last one of the three backbones of the Element Spirit Race, Slade.

Les and Claire were both pure Element Spirits, and they had quite simple forms.

However, Slade was different. He was made up of countless members of the Element Spirit race, who formed a world of their own inside his body. They controlled everything he did.

Chapter 3967 Mark And Offer A Reward The last time when Les wanted to kill Zen straight, Claire rejected him.

Now that she knew that they could never win Zen over, she no longer tried to dissuade Les from doing what he wanted.

"It's a pity that I can't leave now, or I would go to the Grand Pure Realm and burn this guy into ashes," Les muttered.

A few thin lightning bolts clashed with each other as he spoke, which was why his voice seemed laced with the sizzling noise of electric currents.

"We're just watching, but doing nothing?" Claire deadpanned.

As the three backbones of the Element Spirit race, the three of them occasionally received reinforcements.

Those reinforcements also helped them improve their strengths over the years.

They couldn't leave on their own will as of now, and couldn't go to kill Zen.

"I can't get in touch with the Eye Spirit recently. He should have entered the Jade Pure Realm again. It's a bit tricky now..." Claire said with a frown.

She had no hesitation in her the moment she decided to kill Zen. After all, she didn't pity him, though she genuinely wanted him to be on their side.

"Then let the warriors from other races on the Grand Pure Realm do something first," Slade suddenly suggested.

"Warriors of other races?" Les asked. He didn't understand what Slade was talking about.

"Mark and offer a reward," Claire said with a nod.

The two Shadow Warriors listened to Slade's orders, while he formed good relationships with many warriors from various races on the Grand Pure Realm under the Eye Spirit's instruction.

Generally speaking, every race on the Three Purities Stage had their unique theurgies and powers.

An ordinary Eternal Realm warrior who explored the Grand Pure Realm which was the outermost part of the Three Purities Stage was already like a person treading on immensely thin ice. Any warrior from the many races on the Grand Pure Realm was automatically their deadliest opponent.

However, the Element Spirit Civilization had been in the Three Purities Stage for so many years. Although they couldn't subdue all of the races on the Grand Pure Realm, they could still have good relationships with them, as well as exchange interests and make deals with them.

Clatter, clatter, clatter...

At that moment, Slade, who had an armor-like body, suddenly stretched out his hands, and then a white beam of light spread out. At the same time, different treasures appeared one after another.

"It's not easy to make those guys obedient. Offering them the Ghost Tendon? That does not sound good enough. The Dead Sea Glaze? Too unpopular..."

Various treasures flew past the white light in succession.

Even Claire and Les couldn't help but eye the treasures with slight interest.

That was because the Eye Spirit collected most of them. The Eye Spirit usually stored a considerable amount of treasures inside Slade's body.

After all, Slade was not an individual. He could be likened to a city that could move. It was just that members of the Element Spirit race lived in the city. Thus, his current actions represented the decisions of all the members of the Element Spirit race in the city.

"I think I'll just use this oneâ€¦"

In his glowing hands floated some ordinary bone fragments that were about the size of a thumb.

Upon seeing the bone fragments, Claire and Les looked skeptical.

"The Bone Fragments Secret Soul?"

"It's too precious. Will the Eye Spirit even agree?"

The two of them understood that Slade represented the Element Spirit Civilization's Board of Elders to a certain extent, and he had greater rights than Claire and Les. The Eye Spirit usually did not object to any decisions he made.

"That Zen is quite powerful. The warriors of the other races on the Grand Pure Realm are not idiots. Only a great reward will make them brave," said Slade.

Although Claire and Les felt sad at the thought that such a great treasure had to go, they could not interfere.

Once Slade made a decision, he wouldn't change his mind, let alone consider what the two of them thought.

"Buzz!"

When the white light in his hand flashed, he said towards the ice piece, "Shadow Warriors!."

"Yes, sir!" the Shadow Warriors in the ice piece answered.

"Mark Zen," Slade ordered.

"Yes, sir!"

In turn, the two Shadow Warriors stretched out their hands towards Zen simultaneously.

"Buzz..."

Then, two rays of light intersected with each other and formed a distinct mark on Zen's back.

Meanwhile, Zen suddenly felt something as he ran. He turned his head and glanced at the mark.

"What's this?" he asked. "Shadow Mark!" King Ieuan blurted out.

"What's it for?" "The Shadow Mark lasts for about five days after it appears.

During that period, warriors from various races could find your location,"

King Ieuan continued.

Zen frowned deeply. "Can it be removed?" he asked again.

King Ieuan shook its head. "No method can remove it," it said regrettably.

The Shadow Mark was quite well-known in the Grand Pure Realm.

After the appearance of the Shadow Mark, the Element Spirit Civilization would offer a big reward to anyone who could do their bidding. Of course, almost all the warriors from the many races would be interested.

Furthermore, the Shadow Mark would stay permanent for a few days. Even if one fled from the Other Shore, the mark still followed them.

The Snake Goddess, Fuxi, and the others had also heard of it before, but this was the first time they had seen it. All their faces darkened.

However, as soon as King Ieuan finished speaking, Zen's ancestry-level bloodline started to fluctuate. A large, bloody mouth appeared on his back, which was quite near the Shadow Mark. The mouth bit towards it and swallowed it up.

"â€¦â€¦"

King Ieuan looked at the scene, dumbfounded.

"â€¦â€¦"

The Snake Goddess, Fuxi, Eastern Emperor Taiyi, and Yasamin were also speechless.

On the other hand, the two Shadow Warriors that floated in the air looked at each other. They had no idea what had happened.

"The Shadow Mark is something you can't touch, like those two Shadow Warriors. How did you swallow it?" King Ieuan couldn't help but ask.

"Since you swallowed the mark, then that means you could also get rid of the two Shadow Warriors above, right?" the Snake Goddess also asked. A wry smile graced Zen's face as he shook his head.

In truth, the ancestry-level bloodline did things on a whim. Thus, he couldn't control it or make it do what he wanted.

Next to the ice piece in the Supreme Pure Realm stood Slade, who already planned to share the location of the Shadow Mark with the various races.

When the mark disappeared at such a critical moment, he naturally felt enraged. "Shadow Warriors, what are you doing?" he snapped.

"W...we... That Zen had devoured the Shadow Mark!" one of the Shadow Warriors stammered. Clearly, he was immensely afraid of Slade.

"He did eat it..."

"I saw it too."

Claire and Les still watched the ice piece. When they saw the big gap on Zen's back, they were also baffled.

"We can mark the people around him!"

"Yes, that's a good idea!"

Without waiting for Slade to give the order, the two Shadow Warriors once again summoned Shadow Marks.

This time, they aimed at the Snake Goddess and Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

Shadow Marks appeared on the two Eternal Realm warriors' backs almost at once.

When Zen saw that the Shadow Marks appeared again, he tried to remove them for the Snake Goddess and Eastern Emperor Taiyi, but the ancestry- level bloodline sensed that the marks were none of its business. It did not even fluctuate in the slightest, and entirely ignored them.

As soon as the marks had formed completely, the white light in Slade's hand began to spiral. At the same time, a circular white vortex also appeared on the ice piece.

Several large non-human races in the Grand Pure Realm had a huge ice piece inside their places. At this moment, white vortexes also rolled in the center of these ice pieces.

Chapter 3968 Brewing Storm The relationship between the many non-human races of the Grand Pure Realm and the Element Spirit Civilization was strained at best.

The Element Spirit Civilization had been the first ones to be born in the chaos, and were the first to enter the Other Shore.

They had a longer history than most of the other living creatures in the Three Purities Stage.

The many non-human races of the Grand Pure Realm had once fought fiercely with the Element Spirit Civilization. Some powerful races were able to win and maintain their own, separate status. Some had lost and had to submit to the Element Spirit Civilization.

As the Element Spirit Civilization grew stronger and stronger, they began to advance on to the Supreme Pure Realm and then the Jade Pure Realm.

Because of this, many races in the Grand Pure Realm wanted to curry favor with the Element Spirit Civilization.

The Flaming Maple Forest was strong, but the races in it were still hoping to be able to rely on the Element Spirit Civilization's power to help them march onto the Supreme Pure Realm.

Noticing the needs of these other races, the Element Spirit Civilization gave them many ice pieces. If they ever needed these races' help, they would assign the tasks through them. If the tasks were completed, great rewards awaited them.

Many times in the past, the tasks assigned by the Element Spirit Civilization were mainly targeted at those of the Nihility race.

The Nihility race had grown exponentially in the recent years though. When the races first chased down the Nihility race, they had believed them to be weak. However, the Grandmaster of Heaven had easily slaughtered many of them during tasks.

From that point on, everyone was beginning to realize that the Nihility race was as strong as the Element Spirit Civilization. Very few dared to attack them, and the Element Spirit Civilization rarely assigned tasks through the ice pieces anymore.

A burly bull-headed monster lumbered towards the ice piece and stared at it for a long moment. Greed began to glint in his eyes as he exclaimed, "What? The Bone Fragments Secret Soul! I can't believe it!"

The Element Spirit Civilization had always been generous with their rewards, and the treasures they offered were always rare and precious. The Bone Fragments Secret Soul was just that, it was no ordinary item. With the Bone Fragments Secret Soul, they would be able to further strengthen and expand their race. They'd maybe even qualify to enter the Supreme Pure Realm.

A second monster joined the first, eyes wide with shock. "If Slade is willing to offer such a valuable thing as a reward, I can bet you the target is no ordinary creature..."

"Not really! It's just a small group of warriors in the Eternal Realm, measly humans. Nothing to be afraid of!" The monster in front of the ice piece replied.

The humans in the Eternal Realm were nothing to be feared, so the creatures believed. Those of the Grand Pure Realm were only afraid of the Element Spirit Civilization and the Nihility race, as they should be.

The other creature seemed to be a little more cautious. "Why would they need to set such a high price if it was a simple task?" he asked. "There's more to it."

"Of course there's more to it," the first one grunted, turning his head to look over his shoulder at the other. "Apparently, one of these humans just killed Hawley in the Flaming Maple Forest, and left unscathed. That human is the priority target..."

"The group of humans who killed Hawley?!" Someone yelled from behind them.

Several other of their kind were not too far away, shocked by this revelation.

Hawley's death had been shocking news, and spread like wild fire throughout the entirety of the Grand Pure Realm in a matter of days. Those of their race were living closely to the Flaming Maple Forest, so they were the first to know.

The bull-headed creature standing before the ice piece could sense the fear of his kin. "The Misty River race that resides in the forest is incredibly strong," he shouted, "but they are not worthy of being mentioned outside the forest. Even if Hawley was defeated by the human, it only proves he was physically strong. What the fuck are you all afraid of?!"

"You're right! Hawley was untouchable only because he never left the forest. Otherwise, he'd have been eliminated by the Element Spirit Civilization," Another creature chimed in.

"The target has been marked!"

"The other races will also receive notice of this task."

"We have to do something before others decide to..."

The group of monsters were boiling over with excitement.

Meanwhile, the same occurrence was happening among the other races all over the Grand Pure Realm.

The Shadow Warriors had already left marks on the backs of the Snake Goddess and Eastern Emperor Taiyi. This group of humans would be like beacons in the dark to the monsters hunting them from every direction.

The sharp sound of something flying through the air echoed all around.

Zen was zipping through the air at incredible speeds, maintaining the height of ten feet from the ground.

If the Snake Goddess's guidance was right, they should be able to find the entrance by heading north and then west.

There were many different entrances from the Grand Pure Realm to the Supreme Pure Realm. Each one was well designed and full of unknown dangers.

Nearly every non-human creature and Eternal Realm warrior who could enter the Supreme Pure Realm had their own unique methods.

"Those two brats are incredibly annoying!" King Ieuan grumbled as it turned around to look at the two Shadow Warriors flying through the sky.

They were keeping speed with Zen no matter how much faster he attempted to go. It seemed an impossible task to lose them.

"Hey! Look out!"

The Augury Dog beside Fuxi suddenly roared and warned, "There's something coming up ahead, very dangerous!"

He could sense danger with his intuition, although he couldn't tell exactly what kind of danger it was.

Zen squinted, trying to see what was ahead of them. An instant later, a long, thin, green arrow shot towards him.

The arrow was coming at him swiftly like a bolt of lightning.

Fortunately, Zen was always well prepared. With a slight tilt of his body, the arrow narrowly brushed past him.

"More are coming!" The Augury Dog observed.

They whistled through the air as they cut a straight path for them.

More arrows appeared ahead of them, twinkling in the sky like deadly green stars. Simultaneously they all were released and shot towards Zen. They were clumped together in irregular patterns, like a shower of flowers scattered by a fairy.

"Who's firing the arrows?! I can't see anyone." Zen asked.

"It must be the Arrow Demons!" King Ieuan answered. "They use unique arrows that can span across incredibly long distances. Normally, they must aim for the target by eyesight, but since our positions were marked by the Shadow Warriors, they only need to shoot in the direction of the marks."

Zen realized King Ieuan was right. The arrows weren't coming directly for him, they were heading for the Snake Goddess and Eastern Emperor Taiyi on his back. The Arrow Demons couldn't actually see them.

The arrows continued to whistle through the air non-stop. When they were struck, they were destroyed with a loud crack.

Zen was avoiding as many of the arrows as he could, but when he couldn't evade them, he would swing his arm and easily deflect them to the ground.

The arrows seemed to have a mind of their own though. Whenever they would hit the ground, they'd ricochet off and continue their path to the Snake Goddess and Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

It left Zen with no other choice but to reach out and snatch arrows to snap them.

Both the Snake Goddess and Eastern Emperor Taiyi knew the arrows were coming for them, so they were using their theurgies to protect themselves.

The Snake Goddess had wrapped herself in a thick crimson shadow, while Eastern Emperor Taiyi had summoned his golden sword to circle around him.

The sword wouldn't move swiftly until an arrow came too close, then it would snap out and cut the arrow in half.

Despite the mass amount of arrows being rained down on them, very few actually made it near the Snake Goddess and Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

Zen continued his flight, remaining low to the ground. In the face of all the sharp obstacles racing towards him, his speed did not falter.

Chapter 3969 The Jade Bone Arrows About a hundred miles away from Zen, many creatures hung on the vines.

Their bodies had strange shapes and they dangled from the vines entangling the trees.

The lower part of their bodies was shaped like half a gourd. On the upper half were hard bones bending upwards, with golden manes falling from the end of the bones.

The hard bones were bows, and the manes were bowstrings. These short creatures were called Arrow Demons.

They took out many green arrows, and without any hesitation, started shooting them out.

The vine next to the leader of the Arrow Demons had already borne a huge fruit. The fruit looked exactly like an eyeball, with the white sclera and a pupil in the middle. This vine with an eye-shaped fruit was called the Heavenly Eye Vine.

The Heavenly Eye Vine bore a fruit that functioned much better than a normal human eye. It had good eyesight that could see ten thousand miles away.

King Ieuan said that the Arrow Demons used the Shadow Marks to lock them, but its assumption was not completely right. The Arrow Demons also used the eyeball. After they found Zen and his group through the Shadow Marks, it was the eyeball that detected them.

All the Arrow Demons attacked according to what their leader saw.

The relationship between the Arrow Demons and the Heavenly Eye Vine was the same as that of the Misty River race and the Flaming Maple Forest.

They relied on each other to live.

"The Green Willow Arrows don't work on him. He has a very powerful body; no wonder he was able to kill Hawley,"

the leader of the Arrow Demons muttered. He saw Zen move so quickly even as arrows were shot one after another. They didn't stop or slow him down.

The leader's face darkened as he issued an order, "Use the Jade Bone Arrows!"

Hearing the leader's order, the Arrow Demons felt their hearts sink, but they still turned around. They forcefully pulled out the black hard bones extending from their gourd-like bodies.

The process of pulling out the hard bones was excruciating. Some of the Arrow Demons could not help but scream as blood spurted out.

After they had drawn the hard bones from their bodies, black gas began to fume from the bones. They then placed the hard bones on the bows. These bones turned out to be the Jade Bone Arrows that the leader had mentioned.

Every Arrow Demon would grow six black jade bones in their lifetime, and these bones could not be renewed. If all six bones were pulled out, the Arrow Demons would die.

In other words, they were shooting the Jade Bone Arrows at the risk of their lives.

Generally, the Arrow Demons were to use the Jade Bone Arrows when facing a deadly enemy.

However, the reward Slade offered, namely the Bone Fragments Secret Soul, was too tempting. The targets happened to pass by the Arrow Demons' territory, so they were determined not to let them go.

Under the command of the leader, all the Jade Bone Arrows were shot simultaneously.

Suddenly, the leader let out a long and loud roar.

"Woo!"

All the Jade Bone Arrows came to a stop, suspended in the air.

Phew! Phew! Phew! A strange shadow began to appear on one end of the Jade Bone Arrows.

It was a ferocious beast's head, covered with cyan skin, with fangs extending from its snout.

The Arrow Demons had Feather Ghosts' unique bloodline. When the Jade Bone Arrows shot out, the leader had activated their bloodline theurgy.

Whoosh! As the leader's voice shrilled, the long arrows with the Feather Ghosts' heads wailed all over the sky. They shot towards Zen and his group about a hundred miles away.

When the Arrow Demons shifted to use the Jade Bone Arrows, the rain of green arrows halted.

However, Zen did not slow down. The Arrow Demons shot so many arrows towards him; he decided not to let them go.

"Why do the Arrow Demons stop after only three rounds of attacks?"

Eastern Emperor Taiyi asked suspiciously.

"This is not their way of doing things," Yasamin said as she shook her head.

"They are not a powerful race in the Grand Pure Realm. The reason why they gain a foothold in it is that they have very powerful arrows. It is said that these arrows are shot at the expense of their lives..."

As the Snake Goddess spoke, the Augury Dog barked fiercely again.

He would remind them immediately whenever he sensed any danger, but this time, his bark had become wilder.

Then, Zen saw a large group of black dots floating from the distance. They looked like heads with sharp pointed teeth.

"Be careful, Zen. Those are the Jade Bone Arrows,"

the Primeval Lord of Heaven in Zen's mind reminded.

Although Yasamin, the Snake Goddess, and Fuxi had heard of the Arrow Demons before, they had never provoked them. They didn't know much about the Jade Bone Arrows.

"Are they that powerful?" Zen asked.

"They are arrows shot at the cost of the Arrow Demons' lives. They can directly kill their opponents, same as Gerald's Corroding Purple Rain," the Primeval Lord of Heaven explained.

There was a theurgy in the life truth called the Corroding Purple Rain, which was used as a weapon to kill. When the rain fell, it corroded several provinces, eating away all the lives in them.

In the battle against the Pear Hill, Gerald's opponents were the masters at the Eternal Realm. They were strong and thus unafraid that the raindrops could corrode their lives.

However, the Jade Bone Arrows were different. On one hand, they were more powerful than the Corroding Purple Rain; on the other hand, they killed a certain target in unison, unlike the scattered Corroding Purple Rain.

While the group learned the characteristics of the Jade Bone Arrows, the Jade Bone Arrow in front of them shot towards the Snake Goddess.

Almost faster than lightning, Zen grabbed it with his right hand.

He then exerted a powerful force, crushing the Jade Bone Arrow into tiny pieces. However, the Feather Ghost attached to the arrow had bitten into his arm, leaving a small mark.

Swoosh! The Feather Ghost's head disappeared. Zen felt cold rushing through his body as if something had vanished together with the Feather Ghost's head.

Before long, he realized that his life energy was deteriorating.

"Zen, are you okay?" The Snake Goddess keenly sensed that the arrow was not simple.

"Yes, I'm fine."

Zen was confident in his life energy and didn't dwell on it too much.

Facing the dense Jade Bone Arrows, he waved his arms that were thirty feet long and as wide as a wooden bucket.

The Jade Bone Arrows had their own consciousness. They still targeted the Snake Goddess and Eastern Emperor Taiyi on Zen's shoulders. However, when the arrows were damaged, the Feather Ghosts' heads could only attack whoever was nearby.

In a flash, Zen had destroyed dozens of bone arrows, resulting in more Feather Ghosts' heads biting his arms.

Every time a Feather Ghost's head disappeared, he felt his body slowly turn cold, almost like a portion of his life energy was also being taken away.

At first, there hadn't been a noticeable change in his body, but as he shattered more and more bone arrows, his body finally revealed signs of decline.

Wrinkles and black spots were gradually developing on his originally bright and powerful body surface.

For only a short time, Zen had grown from a young man to a middle-aged man, and then to an old man.

Chapter 3970 A Deal "Zen, what's wrong with your body?"

Yasamin was the first one to notice the changes in Zen's body. It was weird and kind of creepy too.

The lifespan of powerful masters like Yasamin and Eastern Emperor Taiyi was limitless. As long as they weren't defeated by some extremely powerful entity, they were essentially immortal.

With such impossible ages, they could change their appearance too.

Yasamin had made herself look like an old person, and Eastern Emperor Taiyi always appeared as a middle-aged man. They had chosen these appearances just to be in charge of the Oneness Sky Palace.

The strange changes in Zen's body were occurring obviously because of those Jade Bone Arrows.

"The bone arrows are taking his life... They are sucking his existence from within him!" The Snake Goddess frowned.

Zen's life energy was being crazily devoured, and his speed, strength, reaction capacity and so many other factors were all being reduced significantly.

Whoosh! Four Jade Bone Arrows found a gap between Zen's hands and shot straight towards Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

Eastern Emperor Taiyi sat down cross-legged in a flash and gently pointed with his finger. His sword immediately spiraled over and slashed at the Jade Bone Arrows.

Crack! The arrows were instantly slashed into two and fell down. However, the Feather Ghosts attached to them were not defeated. They dashed towards Eastern Emperor Taiyi and there was no way to dodge them.

Before Eastern Emperor Taiyi had time to react, the Feather Ghosts bit him and disappeared. Immediately, Eastern Emperor Taiyi turned from a middle-aged man into a very old man with white hair and ragged breathing.

From his condition, it seemed that he would be dead very soon.

"Impossible!"

"I didn't know the Jade Bone Arrows were so powerful. How's Zen doing that?"

"He's been hit by so many arrows and yet he lives..."

Seeing that Zen had withstood about three hundred arrows till now, Fuxi, the Snake Goddess, and the others had come to the conclusion that although the Jade Bone Arrows were quite powerful, they were still not as terrifying as they had heard of them to be.

Unexpectedly, Eastern Emperor Taiyi was already at his last gasp after being hit by just four arrows! And Zen was still fighting.

Just how strong was the life energy of the latter? "Zen... Let's leave the Other Shore first! Squeak!" King Leuan said anxiously.

"There are too many bone arrows here. I'm afraid they will kill us all," the Snake Goddess also reminded him.

Previously, they had all insisted on not retreating from the Other Shore because they had already been marked. Even if they left the Other Shore and hid somewhere temporarily, they would still be at the risk of being pulled back. As long as the enemy was waiting for them, retreating from the Other Shore was much more dangerous than staying here.

But now that they were facing those Jade Bone Arrows, they would be killed anyway if they didn't leave the Other Shore.

Even the Primeval Lord of Heaven advised, "That's right! We'd better retreat at least for now. It would be unrealistic to pin the hopes on your bloodline."

Hearing that, Zen nodded silently.

Then the Augury Dog swiftly drilled into Fuxi's spirit beast bag, while everyone else recited the Illusion Breaking Rune and retreated quickly from the Other Shore.

Zen wasn't too worried. He knew that it would be a piece of cake for the ancestry-level bloodline to replenish the life energy inside him.

The trouble, however, was that the bloodline was not under Zen's own control, and sometimes, it wouldn't be as effective as it should be. It was all up to the bloodline's mood. At the moment, he had no choice but to retreat.

They returned to the Pear Hill once again. The white-haired Eastern Emperor Taiyi was unable to hold on any longer and fell to the ground with a plop like dead meat.

His life energy had been used up and he was on the very verge of death.

The Snake Goddess stretched out her hand and gently brushed the air. A dark green pill appeared out of nowhere on her fingertips, immediately turning into a beam of green light and entering the body of Eastern Emperor Taiyi. However, with the damage the latter had suffered, this wasn't going to be enough.

"Go and ask Gerald to come over here now!" the Snake Goddess said in a hurry.

Without any delay, Fuxi moved away in a flash.

After a short while, Gerald's huge figure suddenly appeared in the sky, emitting green light and looking like a green sun.

Buzz! Two green light columns shot out from his two pincers.

The columns fell down on Eastern Emperor Taiyi who gradually became strong once again. His white hair quickly turned black in front of their very eyes and his body was filled with vitality once again.

"Thank you, Master Gerald," Eastern Emperor Taiyi said as he cupped his hands towards the air in a show of gratitude.

Gerald did not respond. Instead, he turned around and shot two more light pillars towards Zen.

Buzz, buzz, buzz...

The light columns shone on Zen's body. A long time passed but no major change was visible! This was unusual! Gerald's eyes narrowed slightly and he immediately understood what was going on.

It wasn't that his life truth didn't work. But the problem was that the life energy which Zen had consumed was too much for him to recover in a short while. His body was like a bottomless abyss now, and it wasn't going to be easy to fill it up again.

Gerald naturally wouldn't give up. He concentrated and more and more life energy was continuously infused into Zen's body.

On the Other Shore The Jade Bone Arrows didn't fall down after being unable to find their targets anymore. Instead, they were dragged on by the Feather Ghosts and circled around the place where Zen and the others had been just moments ago.

The Arrow Demons were not surprised at the sudden disappearance of Zen and his companions. They knew that the Eternal Realm warriors who came from the chaos would usually use this means to flee when in too much danger.

In order to counteract this, the creatures on the Other Shore would often prepare the Soul Interdicting Water and use it to lock their targets. However, this time, the incident had happened all of a sudden, and the Arrow Demons hadn't gotten a chance to apply the Soul Interdicting Water on their bodies.

Crack! Crack! Crack...

Numerous Arrow Demons were hanging on the green vines. Suddenly, the vines pierced through the ground and advanced forwards at an astonishing speed.

The Arrow Demons had almost no ability to move. They had to rely one hundred percent on the Heavenly Eye Vine to move.

Pretty soon, using the vines, the Arrow Demons arrived at the place where Zen and the others had disappeared. Once again, the Heavenly Eye Vine grew crazily, and completely surrounded the area.

At the same time, the leader of the Arrow Demons spoke to a hill which was located nearby, "There's no point in hiding! The refracting skill is a mere trick. You cannot avoid being discovered by the heavenly eye!"

At his words, a twisted space suddenly appeared at the back of the hill. As it gradually took shape, three figures with the similar appearance to Norris' appeared. These were members of the Gear race! "Gah, Gah..."

As soon as the three members of the Gear race showed up, every single arrow was suddenly placed on the bowstrings by the Arrow Demons and pointed at them.

"We're not looking for trouble." The leader of these members of the Gear race raised both of his hands. Then, he continued, "Look. You've already caught the targets and can obtain the bounty, right?"

"It is none of your business," the leader of the Arrow Demons replied coldly.

Dozens of Jade Bone Arrows were still circling around in the sky, and below them was a thorny cage made of the Heavenly Eye Vine. The Arrow Demons were totally sure that they could catch Zen and his companions this time.

"But you still have one last step left." The man of the Gear race made a gesture of grabbing something in the air. "They are outside the Other Shore.

We'll bring them back. In return, all we want is one third of the Bone Fragments Secret Soul."

The leader of the Arrow Demons was not happy at all with this bargain. He replied in a cold voice, "Do you think only members of your Gear race can do this task? That's too much to ask!"

The member of the Gear race chuckled and replied, "You can ask help from the members of the Sickle race as well, but Zen is definitely not an ordinary Eternal Realm warrior. His physical body is astonishingly strong. Even some of the most powerful warriors of our Gear race won't be able to hold on for a single round during a fight with him, and his life energy is too much to drain, which means his recovery speed is also astonishing. It won't be long before he regains his life energy. Do you have the confidence to deal with him on your own?"

The leader of the Arrow Demons fell silent at this question.

He had spent so many Jade Bone Arrows already and had forced Zen to reach his limit, like a spent arrow. If what the member of the Gear race was saying was true, it would be a pity if he were to be stingy now.

"One fifth," said the leader of the Arrow Demons firmly.

"One-fourth," replied the member of the Gear race.

"Alright! Deal!"

As soon as the leader of the Arrow Demons finished speaking, the thorny vines that had formed the prison rolled around and created a path.

Chapter 3971 Inexhaustible Life Energy From the top of the Heavenly Eye Vine, the leader of the Arrow Demons squinted at the three figures in the distance.

The Jade Bone Arrows that spiraled in the air resembled vultures circling over their prey.

The Arrow Demons were unwilling to give the Bone Fragments Secret Soul to the Gear race. The plan was once the members of the Gear race brought back the targets, they'd let the Jade Bone Arrows rain.

The Jade Bone Arrows were deadly. There was no way the targets or the members of the Gear race would come out of this alive.

The Arrow Demons had lived with the Heavenly Eye Vine for so long.

They not only relied on their powerful archery skills for survival, but also their ruthlessness.

However, the three members of the Gear race didn't make a move after they entered the center. The one in the lead suddenly raised his head and announced, "We just swallowed the Exploding Fire Essence."

Upon hearing this, the leader and the other Arrow Demons were all stunned.

"Don't worry. As long as we're unhurt, they won't explode," he added.

The Arrow Demons and the Heavenly Eye Vine trembled in fear. They were most afraid of the Exploding Fire Essence. If they set off the explosion of the Exploding Fire Essence, they would be doomed.

The three members of the Gear race eyed the Arrow Demons in the distance warily. When they were sure that they were in the clear, they began to look for Zen's shadow.

It was clear to them that although Eastern Emperor Taiyi and the Snake Goddess bore the marks of the Element Spirit Civilization, the main target was that giant human.

Orange lights flashed in their palms. Together, they grabbed at Zen's shadow which was projected on the Other Shore.

Meanwhile, in the Pear Hill, Gerald was rapidly infusing life energy into Zen's body.

As the Chaos Ancient God in charge of the life truth, his life energy was the strongest. It was easy for him to extract it through his bloodline, providing a steady supply of life energy for Zen.

However, it still cost Gerald quite a lot just to revive Zen.

From an old man, Zen suddenly reverted to being middle aged, then gradually, he returned to his youthful self. Around ninety percent of his life energy had been replenished when suddenly, his eyes rolled to the back of his head and he collapsed to the ground.

"What's wrong?"

"Why did he faint?"

"He has been pulled to the Other Shore," the Snake Goddess said once she figured it out.

Everyone was well aware of the situation on the Other Shore. The Arrow Demons were not going to let them go. Not only would they be unable to help Zen, if they rashly returned to the Other Shore, they might even cause more trouble for him.

In the Grand Pure Realm, the three members of the Gear race were all stunned to see Zen have almost completely recovered.

The Arrow Demons and the Heavenly Eye Vine were also surprised.

The amount of Zen's life energy that had been consumed was astronomical.

How was it possible he recovered so quickly? Zen locked eyes with the three members of the Gear race who trembled before him. With a shrug, Zen smiled at them. "You never learn your lesson.

Why do you always help those whom you shouldn't have helped?"

"Let's go!"

"Retreat!"

"Leave!"

The three members of the Gear race, immediately realizing something was wrong, attempted to retreat quickly.

Zen, of course, wasn't planning on letting them go that easily.

Planting his foot firmly on the ground, he launched himself towards them, racing towards them like a bull. In the blink of an eye, he had pounced on the last member of the Gear race, pinning him to the ground.

When the other two members realized what had happened, they pressed onward with no hesitation. In their eyes, Zen killing their companion bought them some time to get away.

But to their horror, when they looked back, Zen had stomped on their companion's head, and was already heading towards them.

In two strides, Zen already caught up to the other two.

Boom! Boom! Zen drew an arc in the air. Using only his palm, he sliced the heads off of the two members of the Gear race. Their heads rolled on the ground, their expressions frozen in fear. A few moments later, their lifeless bodies collapsed to the ground.

Swoosh! Swoosh! While this was happening, the Heavenly Eye Vine, along with the Arrow Demons, had fled quickly.

"Those liars! They didn't swallow the Exploding Fire Essence!" the leader of the Arrow Demons roared angrily.

On the one hand, they were putting distance between them and Zen; on the other, they were so afraid that the Exploding Fire Essence would be activated, so they immediately took off. To their surprise, even with the three members of the Gear race dead, there were no explosions.

"Well then..." The leader of the Arrow Demons suddenly let out a long roar.

The Jade Bone Arrows that had been circling in the air all suddenly shot towards Zen.

At the same time, under Zen's feet, many sharp thorny vines broke through the soil and wrapped around him.

Da! Da! Da! Those Jade Bone Arrows were unable to pierce through Zen's tough skin and became blunt. However, the Feather Ghosts that were attached to the arrows drilled into his body one after another.

"Everyone, please offer your black jade bones!"

There weren't many black jade bones left for the Arrow Demons, but they had no other choice at the moment. They had to take Zen down at any cost, or they would be doomed.

The Heavenly Eye Vine also knew this. It continued wrapping its branches around Zen, layer by layer.

However, Zen just calmly shook his body slightly, breaking off all the thorns. He raised his arms fiercely, breaking off the vines as he did.

As soon as the vines fell to the ground, a volley of Jade Bone Arrows showered over him.

The Arrow Demons were desperate. For some, giving up their last black jade bone meant death, yet they still offered it to their companions. They were willing to sacrifice themselves to kill Zen.

With countless Jade Bone Arrows attacking Zen, it took a toll on his body.

Zen began to age quickly.

In the meantime, from the Pear Hill, everyone could see what was happening. Immediately, Gerald leaped into action and extended a pair of pincers, replenishing Zen's life energy once more.

More and more Arrow Demons fell as they offered their last arrows, while Gerald consumed the power of life truth.

Under the rain of arrows, Zen flew up to the nearest vine and grabbed it.

Clasping the vine in both hands, he shook it violently. The small Arrow Demons all fell to the ground. Swiftly, Zen squashed them all with just one finger.

The Arrow Demons could only put up a fight from afar using their archery skills, as face-to-face combat proved fatal to them.

Desperately, he looked at Zen with pleading yet disbelieving eyes. On his way up, Zen had already been pierced by around five hundred Jade Bone Arrows, yet he still glowed youthfully. Such a feat was inconceivable.

Chapter 3972 The Whining Road Zen looked at the leader of the Arrow Demons indifferently. Then, he stretched out his right hand in a flash.

Before the leader could even try to beg for mercy, he was smashed into a cloud of blood.

As the eye sensed that it was in grave danger, a purple vine as thick as a finger suddenly extended towards Zen. When it touched him, a strand of consciousness was transmitted to him. "Yes, I can speak. Please don't hurt me."

The voice sounded like a human woman's. Moreover, it sounded very weak.

Zen could sense that the Heavenly Eye Vine had a strong desire to live.

"You were trying to kill us just now. What makes you think you deserve to live?" Zen asked harshly.

The situation in the Three Purities Stage was extremely chaotic. Even the Element Spirit Civilization did not implement any rules here. Although the creatures of different races were intelligent, they followed the law of the jungle: kill, or be killed.

The Heavenly Eye Vine realized that it couldn't fool Zen. A vine grew from its eye. The vine extended towards Zen to reveal a small tender sprout on its tip.

"This sprout is my source of life," the Heavenly Eye Vine admitted.

Although it was a plant, it was good at discerning people. It knew that if it refused to tell Zen, then Zen would kill it on the spot.

In order to survive, how could it dare to hide anything? Zen reached out his hand to touch the source of life of the Heavenly Eye Vine, and he could feel its vigorous life energy. He could even read its memories. The Heavenly Eye Vine spoke the truth. This small sprout indeed controlled its life and death.

Although they knew clearly how powerful Zen was, the creatures in the Three Purities Stage on the Other Shore had different methods. In addition to sucking Zen's life energy, there were many other methods. Naturally, they were still a little worried.

Splash! Splash! The Heavenly Eye Vine's head looped around a bit before it extended towards the Snake Goddess and Fuxi. Then, Zen popped out from above and said excitedly, "Please, come up!"

"Come up?" Yasamin frowned.

The Arrow Demons were tyrannical. Normally, few creatures could get close to them, so even the Snake Goddess didn't know that much about them.

After everyone climbed onto the vine, Zen used the big eye to look around.

The eye had good eyesight, and it could see everything within a radius of ten thousand miles.

On the other side of the Flaming Maple Forest, there was some sort of a commotion. Upon a closer look, Zen realized many flying snakes with transparent wings were heading straight for him.

On the southwest side, dozens of tall and sturdy bull-headed men carried golden axes and were steadily making their way over.

On the northwest side...

The creatures in the Grand Pure Realm were not easy to deal with. They each had an extraordinary ability. It had taken Zen a lot of energy to deal with the Arrow Demons alone. If these creatures were to besiege Zen and his group, the situation would look dim.

Zen ordered the Heavenly Eye Vine.

Although the Heavenly Eye Vine was only a plant, it moved surprisingly fast.

Previously, it was over a hundred miles away from Zen, but it carried a group of Arrow Demons and rushed to him very quickly.

Chapter 3973 Interceptor Every Eternal Realm warrior that could enter the Supreme Pure Realm had their own unique methods.

Slade was not an individual. When the many members of the Element Spirit race expressed their feelings through him, it was like a torture to Les.

There was a wide passage at the bottom of the Dual Topknot Mountain.

This passage was in the north of the Grand Pure Realm and was called the Silent Path by the members of various races.

The Silent Path was safe. As long as one followed the rules, they wouldn't be attacked or be in danger.

But as the name of the passage suggested, people had to keep absolutely silent while passing through the Silent Path and not make any sound.

Silence was the biggest rule here.

A few fist-sized creatures floated in the air along the Silent Path. These creatures were shaped like jellyfish, looked cottony, and were light as air.

They floated in every corner of the Silent Path at all times of the day.

These white flocculent creatures belonged to the Mystical Void race.

The Mystical Void creatures weren't all that intelligent. They fed on space and never contacted the outside world. It was difficult for people from the outside world to capture or interfere with them.

Some even maintained that the members of the Mystical Void race were not living beings, but just another form of space.

The biggest weakness of the Mystical Void race was their cowardice. Any loud noise would spook them and they'd immediately transform from the flocculent form into the space form.

In their space form, they were compressed together and had once crushed many warriors of different races into dust. Only a small number of people could still walk out of the Silent Path after provoking the Mystical Void race.

After Slade gave the order, six nonhuman warriors arrived at the Silent Path.

They were silent as they flew along the Silent Path.

Every dozens of miles, they had placed a silver tube that looked like a whistle on the ground. This way, there were a large number of tubes along the way.

They had walked through the entire Silent Path when one of the warriors reached out a hand and gently pressed the tube at the end.

The silver tube suddenly began to whistle a harsh, keening sound.

The Silent Path was eerily quiet, and the sudden whistling sound was particularly shrill and loud.

Buzz, buzz, buzz...

A creature of the Mystical Void race above the silver tube shook violently, its cotton-like body beginning to expand and turning into a milky white space that expanded in all directions.

The space grew larger by ten times, a thousand times, a million times! As the space expanded, it crashed into the bodies of the six warriors, sending them flying.

The silver tubes in the Silent Path began to whistle in unison, the sound even louder than before.

The usually quiet Silent Path became so noisy that almost all the members of the Mystical Void race were surprised. Their bodies began to swell and they began to turn into the space forms.

These huge spaces squeezed and merged with each other.

It looked like countless bubbles merging together, forming a peculiar golden color.

When the six warriors stood up from the ground and saw this, their hearts still fluttered with fear.

If they remained in the Silent Path, they would be squeezed into meat paste by these space bubbles.

When the members of the Mystical Void race were frightened, they'd become like this for a full month, which meant that the Silent Path would be closed for a month and that the task that Slade had given to the six warriors could be considered completed.

Whoosh, whoosh, whoosh...

The Heavenly Eye Vine emerged from the ground like a snake and dived back into the ground. This happened multiple times, completely destroying the soil along the way.

It was not, however, a big deal for the Eternal Realm warriors present.

"You're courting death," Zen warned.

Chapter 3974 Eternal Realm Hunters As soon as Zen was sucked into the black hole, the two Eternal Realm warriors let go of each other's hands, and the black hole disappeared! They smiled as though they had won an incredible prize.

It was hard to fathom the truth of what the Snake Goddess said, since they had not seen Claire or the Grandmaster of Heaven defeated with their own eyes.

"Why else do you think is the Element Spirit Civilization so determined to kill us? Even at the cost of the Bone Fragments Secret Soul?" the Snake Goddess asked coolly.

In the eyes of the three Eternal Realm Hunters, this task was extremely simple.

Zen was obviously the most powerful in his group.

The Element Spirit Civilization had used the ice piece to pass its orders and tasks to other creatures. Somehow, the Eternal Realm Hunters had managed to get their hands on an ice piece, through which they received the current task. They then conducted an investigation and learned that Zen had massive physical strength, and that he had killed Hawley in the Flaming Maple Forest.

Thus, based on what the Eternal Realm Hunters knew about the Flaming Maple Forest, Zen had a stronger body than Hawley.

However, the Eternal Realm Hunters weren't afraid of a powerful body or physical strength alone. Without the suppression of the Flaming Maple Forest, they thought it would not be difficult for them to kill Zen using their theurgies.

The task proved as simple as they had anticipated. Zen had no time to fight back before he fell into the Black Sun of Sawyer and Thurston.

No matter how strong one was and what special abilities they had, they could never pass through an exit that did not exist.

For instance, once in the Supreme Pure Realm, the three Eternal Realm Hunters had encountered the immortal Cyan Bone Ghosts, and used the Black Sun on them.

It was said that the ninety-nine Cyan Bone Ghosts in the Supreme Pure Realm never died. They had wandered aimlessly for a long time in the Supreme Pure Realm, killing countless creatures who crossed their paths.

The Element Spirit Civilization and the Nihility race had been unable to deal with them, and instead evaded the Cyan Bone Ghosts when they encountered them.

They had never imagined that someone could survive after being devoured by the Black Sun. It was too strange to even consider.

The movements of the two halves were coordinated. Obviously, they belonged to a single being, although an invisible space in the middle still separated them as they crawled out.

The two halves of the Black Sun exerted an irresistible gravitational force upon each other. Independent of any action by Sawyer and Thurston, the two black semicircles drew closer and closer to each other, dragging the two brothers towards one another.

Finally, the two halves met, and the Black Sun was formed. As the circle became whole, so did the two halves of the body, joining together to form a single human shape.

A space fluctuation appeared above them, accompanied by a flash of golden light. For a split second, everything was silent until a huge, golden axe suddenly emerged and hacked down towards them! Fortunately, the Heavenly Eye Vine was prepared and twisted its body to the side to avoid the attack. The golden axe hit the ground instead of the vine and left behind a shining, golden crack.

Flames blazed within the crack but seemed to be unable to burn the ground.

"It doesn't matter where they are. We should climb up to the top of the Sky Ladder Plateau first," Zen suggested.

With Zen's command, the Heavenly Eye Vine twisted its body and quickly fled the place.

Buzz...

Of course, there was no way their escape was going to be so easy. As the Heavenly Eye Vine fled, another space fluctuation appeared above them as two golden axes dropped down at the same time.

There was nothing the Eternal Realm Hunters could really do but stare nervously at Zen and wait for his fate to consume him.

Sure enough, the small golden flames quickly spread from the sharp edge of the axe and onto Zen's arm as it burned his flesh with a sizzling sound.

Zen's virtually indestructible body quickly crumpled and charred under the onslaught of the flames but still, he remained standing.

"Do you want to burn me to nothing but ashes?" he muttered. The flames continued to lick at his skin but Zen continued to carry the axe with both hands.

Once caught in the flames, the fire would only continue to spread along the victim's body faster and faster.

If this went on, Zen would definitely be burned to nothing, including the ancestry-level bloodline inside his body.

Up until now, the only way Zen was able to use this formidable ancestrylevel bloodline he obtained was by putting himself in danger. If he helped his friends but did not put his own safety in question, then the bloodline would never activate.

In a real predicament like this one, he was sure that the ancestry-level bloodline would rise up and protect itself! Buzz! Sure enough, Zen's shoulder suddenly swelled and formed a big sac that exploded and turned into a monstrous, gaping mouth with sharp teeth! "Okay, here it goes," Zen murmured to himself.

He could only sigh at the sight of the ugly mouth on his shoulder.

The ancestry-level bloodline was truly powerful and Zen had yet to see any limits or weaknesses to it.

However, every time it showed off its power, it seemed to always attach a gruesome and somewhat terrifying addition to his body.

Whoosh! Whoosh! Everyone watched as this monstrous mouth that suddenly grew on his shoulder sucked and devoured the Life Devouring Flames, including those that burned on the axe blade.

Once all of the flames had been eaten, the golden axe became nothing more than an ordinary chunk of sharp metal.

All Zen needed to do was exert a bit of strength before he was able to snap the huge axe in half! Everyone who witnessed this scene almost had their eyes pop right out of their sockets in surprise.

'What is with that weird mouth that suddenly grew on his shoulder? How was that mouth able to devour the flames so easily?' they all couldn't help but wonder to themselves.

Among the three Eternal Realm Hunters, Pearson was the most knowledgeable and also most scheming.

When he saw what had happened, he surmised that Zen's body was able to adjust itself to all sorts of predicaments.

So did that mean that he had also sorts of method that could correspond to defeating other theurgies? If that was the case then wouldn't that make him entirely omnipotent? It was merely a conjecture since Pearson had no way to prove it. Who knows? Maybe it was mere coincidence that Zen's body had the ability to restrain the Life Devouring Flames.

However, he remembered the fact that Zen was also able to escape from the Black Sun with a strange physical form. Was that also a coincidence then? There seemed to be too many coincidences in this world.

Pearson thought it through but couldn't come up with a sound hypothesis as of the moment. 'Maybe Sawyer and Thurston made the right choice to follow him?' he thought to himself.

All of a sudden, more power of space surged across the sky as multiple giant axes began to rain down upon them in succession! Chapter 3980 A Trick The Heavenly Eye Vine was a monster that had lived for countless years.

Only those who'd made a great contribution would be awarded with a second Golden Spirit Axe.

The bull-headed men who came here were the most powerful elites of their race. Many of them had two Golden Spirit Axes, and some even had three.

The width of the fifth stair of the Sky Ladder Plateau was less than a tenth of that of the first stair, and the sixth stair was even narrower. On the other side of the Sky Ladder Plateau, a large number of creatures from other races began to pour in. More and more races joined the chase.

They didn't cooperate with each other as the Eternal Realm Hunters thought. Time was short and they hated each other very much. Although everyone's goal was to catch Zen and his group, they were also still wary against each other.

Even two races that were approaching together maintained a considerable distance from each other.

Clatter! Clatter! Clatter! The temperature at the top of the Sky Ladder Plateau started to drop. Thick snow had piled up on the plain, covering everything in a blanket of white.

After passing the sixth stair, the Heavenly Eye Vine climbed up rapidly along the mountain sides of the seventh.

The three Eternal Realm Hunters, the Snake Goddess, Fuxi and the others now looked a little nervous.

If the wind blew from the Purple Wind Gorge, the Sky Ladder Plateau would be a dead end. There would be no possibility of escape.

After the Heavenly Eye Vine reached the seventh stair, Thurston, Sawyer, Fuxi and the Snake Goddess held their breath and looked worriedly ahead.

The Snake Goddess frowned. This was a difficult problem she could find no solution for.

A feeling of doom hung over Eastern Emperor Taiyi, Yasamin and the Eternal Realm Hunters.

They couldn't cross the Purple Wind Gorge if the wind raged at them.

All the creatures in the air would be sucked into the deep gorge, and there was no possibility of survival.

The wind in the Purple Wind Gorge was famously insurmountable.

Since Zen and his group were wanted by the Element Spirit Civilization, they knew they were definitely not weak.

"You destroyed the Diabolic Earth and killed my clansmen, you brat! You'll pay for that today!" One of the Diabolic Demons took two steps forward, looking like he could swallow Zen in one gulp.

When the other creatures heard this, their expressions changed slightly.

The Diabolic Earth was now as quiet as death. No one dared to go and have a look, so only a few people knew about it.

"Humph!" The Diabolic Demons didn't answer.

"Did they destroy it?" the giant pressed.

"Yes! It's that brat!" The king gritted his teeth and pointed at Zen.

Hearing this, the creatures started to stir uncomfortably.

The Diabolic Demons were among the top three most powerful races in the Grand Pure Realm. It was near impossible to kill them.

All this time, they thought Zen, who had defeated Hawley, just had a powerful physique.

It seemed that the information they got was completely inaccurate.

Although surprised at this development, the creatures did not retreat. After all, they still had the advantage of numbers.

"Master Fuxi, please get the Solid Lightning Powder ready."

Chapter 3984 The Stone Spirits Faced with such a dire situation, they had no way of retreating.

These creatures could control several forms of mist, and each of them had a different effect. The red blood mist had the power to confuse the enemy; the yellow poison mist was highly toxic; the green spiritual mist could generate white bones and muscles; the purple mist could corrode everything.

It was undoubtedly not easy to corrode the Stone Spirits. Moreover, the mist creatures hadn't launched a heavy attack this time. Their main goal was to corrode the spider threads wrapped around the Stone Spirits' bodies.

Pearson's body, which was in the form of spider threads, would be corroded into nothingness very soon.

However, as soon as the purple mist was formed, Pearson sensed the danger and immediately pulled back the spider threads to form his body.

Even though his reaction had been extremely fast, the spider threads had broken down at several places. If he had moved just a little later, he would have been completely corroded by the purple mist.

As soon as the spider threads were removed, the Stone Spirits began moving once again.

Chapter 3985 The Green Wind After some of Pearson's threads were corroded, he grew a little weak.

Chapter 3986 Giant Hawk The Bone-coagulating Powder and the Solid Lightning Powder were similar in appearance, but their properties were vastly different.

Chapter 3987 No Turning Back Pearson told the Wing King the story of the Regal Jade Spirit in detail.
