When he had started to decide the route in the beginning, Zen had known that the Wing King had entered the Three Purities Stage from the Regal Jade Spirit in his body. The Civilization Artifact of the Regal Jade Civilization could sense the position of the Wing King.

The Regal Jade Spirit had told Zen with certainty that the Wing King could easily take the group through the Purple Wind Gorge.

Now, it seemed that everything had come through even though there had been a little trouble in the process.

"Did you choose the Whining Road?" the Wing King asked again.

The Wing King had once led many of the Eternal Realm warriors of the Regal Jade Civilization to advance into the Supreme Pure Realm. But they failed when they were four hundred miles from the Supreme Pure Realm.

The Regal Jade Civilization was strong enough. They had merely chosen a different path.

At the time, the Wing King had been in a hurry to prove himself. After entering the Three Purities Stage, he had led his people towards the Supreme Pure Realm through the Flame Road.

The Flame Road was a very difficult road. There were very few people who chose this road to enter the Supreme Pure Realm. At the time, the Wing King had overestimated the strength of the Element Spirit Civilization, which was why he had suffered a great defeat.

If the Wing King hadn't been in a hurry, it would not have been impossible for him to enter the Supreme Pure Realm.

"Yes, Wing King," said the Snake Goddess, folding her hands towards him in respect.

"I've heard that the Whining Road is a dangerous road. Are you sure you will succeed?" the Wing King asked again.

They had failed near the entrance of the Flame Road, which was a pain he would never get rid of in his lifetime. It had made him extremely sensitive to these roads.

"We passed successfully," said Fuxi proudly.

The Wing King nodded, but his expression soon turned gloomy. "That's good. I failed when I had the chance."

"It's not that your strength wasn't enough. You just didn't have a thorough understanding of these roads at the time," the Snake Goddess said, trying to reassure him.

The creatures on the Other Shore knew more about the Three Purities Stage with the passing of time. Just like the mysterious veil had been pulled down bit by bit, the creatures that had later tried had become more familiar with these roads. It would now naturally be easier to pass through them.

"I think I can benefit from your success this time and enter the Supreme Pure Realm with you," the Wing King added.

A smile appeared on the Snake Goddess's face. "Wing King, you are being modest."

Swoosh...

As the wide wings of the Wing King flapped fiercely, the group of people in the purple wind sped up again.

After a few minutes, the Wing King began to rise upwards. He flew upwards for a while before emerging from the purple wind.

Towards everyone's left was a cliff that stretched for thousands of miles. On the right was an endless plain.

Once the Wing King put the Heavenly Eye Vine down, Zen began to look at the scenery in the distance, a strange expression soon crossing his face.

"I'm now standing in the north and facing the south," Zen said, pointing at the plain in front of him. "If I keep going along this plain, won't I reach the south of the Grand Pure Realm?"

To put it more simply, if this plain was the center of the Grand Pure Realm, they could have reached this place if they had gone up along the Divine River and then crossed it after they came out of the Flaming Maple Forest.

They needn't have spent so much effort in going around it.

"That's not a plain," the Snake Goddess said, walking up to him. "It's just an illusion. The entrance is over there."

The Snake Goddess pointed at a place a little distance away.

There were two rows of inconspicuous fences.

A simple entrance sat in between these two rows of fences.

Zen frowned at this sight. The fences weren't remarkable but Zen should have noticed them. The fact that they hadn't struck him was strange.

"If we had walked through the plain, the only road to the Supreme Pure Realm would be through the entrance between these two rows of fences."

The Snake Goddess stretched out her slender fingers and drew a line in the air. "If you don't walk through this road and try to pass through other places on both sides, you will be lost forever in this endless plain."

"Is this illusion that powerful?" Zen raised his eyebrows.

As the Snake Goddess nodded, the Primeval Lord of Heaven's voice rang out in Zen's mind. "This plain is not an illusion!"

"If it weren't an illusion, we could just come out of the plain by retracing our steps. Why would we be lost forever?" Zen asked in his mind.

The Primeval Lord of Heaven chuckled. "Those who enter the plain can no longer turn around. The thoughts of all of the people who enter the plain will change irreversibly and they will lose the ability of turning back."

"Is turning back also a kind of ability?" Zen was speechless.

"Yes, and changing your thoughts doesn't mean modifying your memories.

It's by making you not realize you have this ability of turning around, so that you can only move forward permanently. You know something is wrong, but you will never be able to figure out what it is," the Primeval Lord of Heaven explained, shrugging. "This is indeed a miraculous plain. It can suppress the thoughts and logic of all living beings."

Chapter 3988 Treacherous Beings Zen did not pursue the topic about the plain's magic ability. He went to the entrance, which was two rows of fences, with the others.

The fences seemed to have existed for a long time as they looked utterly decayed.

There were exquisite carvings on the surface of the fences, and they were rotten as well.

Upon closer look, Zen noticed that there was a complete carving on top of a post, but a film of dust covered a part of it. Just as he was about to brush it off, Fuxi looked at him in horror and said, "Zen, don't touch this fence!"

Zen's fingers stopped one inch before the fence and he asked, "Why?"

"There's something ominous about the fences. Anyone who touches them can't get out of the Whining Road," Fuxi said with certainty.

Zen raised one brow. "Is that so?"

He didn't believe Fuxi, but everything was possible on the Other Shore.

Perhaps, the fences did have something to do with the Whining Road.

In the end, he did not touch the fence. At that moment, the Heavenly Eye Vine extended a thin branch and gently touched his forehead, then passed its thoughts to him. "I... I've already sent you here. Can I leave now?" it said.

Zen had forced the Heavenly Eye Vine to come with them, and its life source was still in his hands.

He glanced at the Heavenly Eye Vine's large pupil and said, "As far as I know, you can only go through the Silent Path if you go back from here. Do you think those races will let you go?"

The Heavenly Eye Vine was also a member of those races. The problem was that those warriors had thought that it had shifted to Zen's side.

Even in ordinary times, it was hard for it to survive alone without the Arrow Demons. Now, those races were already enraged at what it did, so the chances of them letting the Heavenly Eye Vine go were quite small.

The vine thought for a while and answered, "No, they won't..."

"Then what's your plan?" Zen asked again. "I...

I'd better follow you... " In reality, the Heavenly Eye Vine didn't want to follow Zen and his group.

After all, the Whining Road was dangerous and full of strange things.

Furthermore, it was hard for it to survive alone due to its current state, even if it did reach the Supreme Pure Realm.

"If everyone is ready, come with us. It is said that the Whining Road is very mysterious and terrifying.

I think everyone here must've known about it except for Zen, right?" Fuxi announced. In turn, Zen's eye twitched and he glared at Fuxi.

"The Whining road is indeed dangerous, but it's actually quite simple once we discover its secret.

That is also why we chose it," Fuxi explained as he turned around and walked towards the road between the two rows of fences. "Everyone, please follow me closely. I'm sure we can pass safely!" he continued.

"Swish, swish, swish..."

The Heavenly Eye Vine immediately followed behind Fuxi. It was afraid of being left behind.

But when it went to the front, the others got squeezed out of the line.

Fuxi looked helplessly at the Heavenly Eye Vine and said, "Do you want to stay in my spirit beast bag?"

Fortunately, his spirit beast bag was large enough to hold the Heavenly Eye Vine.

However, most creatures refused to stay in a spirit beast bag unless the bag's owner was someone they highly trusted.

Perhaps the dangerous Whining Road intimidated the Heavenly Eye Vine so much, that it quickly stretched out a thin vine then touched Fuxi's head, sending him the message that it had agreed to his suggestion.

Afterward, Fuxi released the Augury Dog from the spirit beast bag and put the Heavenly Eye Vine inside it. They also needed the Augury Dog to pass through the Whining Road, and he had planned to release him anyway.

Then, they walked into the path between the fences one after another. The Wing King's body was too large, so he shrunk himself before he proceeded.

Yet, nothing changed after they went in.

There was still the endless plain in the distance. On one side was a cliff, and on the other was the end of the Purple Wind Gorge.

As for the two rows of fences, they were like rows of wood lined up on the plain, which did not mean anything.

But after they traveled some more, a faint white fog appeared around them.

The further they moved, the thicker the white fog was.

Zen looked back and found that both the cliff and the Purple Wind Gorge disappeared.

However, the two rows of fences were still there, and their positions just annoyed them. "The road between the fences is closed?" Zen asked in a low voice.

There were two rows of fences before, but now they became one as if by magic.

"Don't ask," the Snake Goddess hissed.

Just then, her eyes glowed red, as if she tried to infuse the shadow of Snake Goddess into her eyes. He wondered what she saw when she did that.

But since she told him not to ask, he just stayed quiet.

Eastern Emperor Taiyi, Yasamin, and the three Eternal Realm Hunters were also confused, but they followed the Snake Goddess and Fuxi obediently.

They walked for a little more, then a cabin with a spire appeared in the thick fog.

When they got closer, Zen saw that it was a thatched hut.

The thatched hut had no doors, so he couldn't see what was inside.

The moment they approached it, however, they felt extremely uncomfortable.

To the people who had held high positions for a long time like Eastern Emperor Taiyi and Yasamin, the sensation felt like an uncontrollable urge to kill each other.

Still, they were in a mysterious place, so they restrained themselves.

As soon as they passed the thatched hut, everyone could restrict the strange feeling inside them.

However, two more thatched huts appeared in front of them.

All the thatched huts were closed, but the creatures inside had given them an unpleasant feeling.

Driven by curiosity and uneasiness, King Ieuan could not help but ask, "What exactly is inside them?"

"Don't ask," the Snake Goddess stated again.

King Ieuan's soybean-like eyes flashed, but it couldn't do anything but continue to move forward.

When they passed by another neat row of thatched huts again, Pearson suddenly stopped. "You have to tell us what's inside them before we decide to move forward or not," he demanded.

It wasn't that Pearson didn't trust the Snake Goddess, but the Eternal Realm Hunters never pinned all their hopes on others.

Therefore, it was better if they knew things in advance so they could deal with emergencies if there were any.

The Snake Goddess's eyes brimmed with regret. She should have told them the rules first before entering the road, but now it was too late.

"It's a kind of Treacherous Being," she replied.

Upon hearing her answer, Pearson only frowned. He already had a rough guess of what was inside the huts, and when he forced an answer out of the Snake Goddess, he was not surprised.

On the contrary, Sawyer and Thurston blanched in fear, and it was clear that they were afraid.

Meanwhile, Eastern Emperor Taiyi, Yasamin, King Ieuan, and Zen didn't have any reaction.

Even in the Supreme Pure Realm, there weren't many creatures who knew about the existence of "Treacherous Beings." Naturally, those warriors who explored the Grand Pure Realm had never heard of them.

When they saw how Sawyer and Thurston looked, however, they immediately understood that those creatures would be a challenge.

Chapter 3989 A Village Fuxi picked up the Augury Dog when they were passing by the neat row of thatched huts and held him in his arms.

The Augury Dog was sensitive to all kinds of power. Now that they were on the Whining Road, the unpleasant aura around the place was beginning to overwhelm him. He looked sickly and weak.

Every time Fuxi passed by a thatched hut with the dog in his arms, his glassy eyes glinted with obvious hostility.

He probably understood that the things in the thatched huts were too strong for them, so he dared not bark wildly. Instead, he whimpered, trying not to let his voice be obvious.

The Augury Dog continued to whimper as they walked past the first row of thatched huts.

When they reached the end of the first row, Fuxi whispered to him, "Is there a thatched hut available for us?"

The Augury Dog shook his head.

Fuxi and the Snake Goddess exchanged a worried glance.

When they had entered the Whining Road the last time, they had found a thatched hut in the front row pretty easily.

Their luck seemed to have run out this time. All twenty-six thatched huts in the first row were occupied.

"Let's try the second row!"

Fuxi knew there was no time for them to lose. He hurriedly went to the second row with the Augury Dog in his arms.

There were a lot of thatched huts in the second row as well. As before, the Augury Dog sniffed at each thatched hut and tried to find a safe place for them to stay.

But they combed through the second row and the Augury Dog still couldn't find an unoccupied hut.

The Snake Goddess blinked but didn't say a word, while Fuxi's face darkened. "The third row then!" he growled.

The others following them remained silent, but they began to become more worried with every passing minute.

It was true that Fuxi and the Snake Goddess had once made their way to the Supreme Pure Realm through this path. But their previous success now seemed to have stemmed out of sheer luck.

And luck didn't seem to be on their side this time.

If they couldn't find an available thatched hut this time, things would become hard for them â€” even harder than being under siege on the top of the Sky Ladder Plateau.

There were seven rows of thatched huts in this area, like a large village in a savage land.

Fuxi took the Augury Dog along to check on every thatched hut in the remaining five rows, but to no avail. His face looked ghastly pale, as if he was terribly ill.

"It's getting late. The sky is much darker now," Zen reminded them, looking up at the sky.

This area was covered in white mist and it was hard to tell the time, but it was obvious that the sunlight had dimmed.

Fuxi looked up, alert at this news, anxiety coursing through him.

They would be in great trouble once night fell.

Fuxi looked like an ant in a hot pot and the Snake Goddess took it upon herself to console him in a calm, soft voice. "There are more huts scattered around here. Let's check each of them out. There's no hurry, Fuxi. We still have time."

The thatched huts in the middle of this area weren't the only ones. There were many others on the periphery.

Drawing comfort from the Snake Goddess's words, Fuxi took a deep breath and nodded. He then walked towards the scattered thatched huts with the Augury Dog.

He examined one thatched hut after the other but the result disappointed him yet again.

The sky was already dark, night drawing close.

"Since we need an unoccupied thatched hut, why don't we work together to drive the Treacherous Being in one of the huts away? Why should we go to all this trouble to find an empty one?" Eastern Emperor Taiyi grumbled impatiently, unable to stand it anymore.

He thought that no matter how powerful the Treacherous Beings were, it wouldn't be a problem for them to tackle them.

Even discounting Zen, all the warriors present were collectively a force to be reckoned with in the Three Purities Stage.

However, Eastern Emperor Taiyi had barely finished talking when a deep, angry howl suddenly sounded from the nearest thatched hut.

It was hard to tell whether the voice was male or female. The howl seemed to contain an extraordinary magical power, causing everyone to cover their ears.

More shrill wails followed the first howl, each emanating from a different thatched hut. The Treacherous Beings had begun to wake up in succession.

"Oh no!"

The Augury Dog in Fuxi's arms whimpered, terrified.

"There are several more thatched huts over there. We can give them a try,"

the Snake Goddess pointed at a corner. There were six or seven thatched huts in the direction she was pointing.

Fuxi didn't hesitate this time. He strode up to them, the Augury Dog still whimpering in his arms.

The Augury Dog tried hard to quell his fear and sniff at each hut. When Fuxi passed by the third hut on the left, his eyes suddenly lit up with hope.

"Thank God! This one is empty! Let's go in!"

Zen, Eastern Emperor Taiyi, and the others were anxious as they followed.

But the Augury Dog's words were instant in cheering all of them up.

Fuxi lifted the flap of the hut and hurried inside, the others following closely behind.

The thatched hut was almost as tall as the shrunken Wing King, but it was still barely tall enough to let him in. Upon noticing this, the Wing King had to shrink himself further. Only then did he dive into the hut.

Fuxi didn't close the flap until the Wing King had entered the hut.

All of a sudden, the piercing howls that had lingered for so long in everyone's ears died out. And thanks to this, the discomfort that had haunted everyone was now finally gone.

There was nothing inside the thatched hut apart from a wooden pillar at its center.

This pillar, pockmarked with several fist-sized holes, seemed to have existed for a long time and looked like it would fall apart at any time.

"The Whining Road is worthy of its name. It's terrifying enough even though we haven't encountered anything yet," King Ieuan commented solemnly.

"Well, we wouldn't be talking like this if we had encountered something,"

said Fuxi with a wry smile.

Yasamin breathed a sigh of relief before she asked, "How long will it take us to pass through the Whining Road?"

"Thirty-two hours make for a day on the Whining Road. We only need to stay here for about three days," the Snake Goddess replied.

Zen had zoned out and had been staring at the pillar. At the Snake Goddess's words, he looked around, his eyebrows raised, and said, "We only need to stay safe for three days?"

The Snake Goddess nodded. "That's all, yes. We'll stay here for three days and after that, we'll return the way we came. We'll then be able to enter the Supreme Pure Realm."

"I didn't know the Whining Road is such an easy path!" Thurston was surprised at the rules. The Eternal Realm Hunters had their own way to reach the Supreme Pure Realm.

In fact, they had more than one way.

But no matter which path they took, they would have to expend full courage and strength.

In contrast, the Whining Road seemed too easy.

"It can't be this simple," Sawyer said, shaking his head. "If this was the case, many more creatures and Eternal Realm warriors would've chosen this path and this path wouldn't be called the strangest of all. Don't forget that there are a bunch of Treacherous Beings outside."

At the mention of the Treacherous Beings, it was as if the light was turned down, given how everyone's faces paled, their hearts sinking within them.

"What on earth is a Treacherous Being?" King Ieuan asked curiously.

Except for Fuxi, the Snake Goddess, and the three Eternal Realm Hunters, no one else knew what their enemies on the Whining Road were or what a Treacherous Being was.

"They have no specific form. They-" The Snake Goddess paused, trying to think up the correct word to describe them. After a while, she said, "It doesn't matter. When it gets darker, you'll be able to see them with your own eyes."

Chapter 3990 Howls It was already dusk and the village was being engulfed by darkness little by little.

Earlier, some rays of light were strongly shooting into the thatched hut. But as the sun went down, the small hut was also enveloped in darkness.

Fortunately, everyone possessed good eyes that they could still use to see their surroundings clearly, even in the pitch darkness.

"Waah! Waah!"

Soon after, loud howls were heard outside.

Just then, a ball of light was seen not far away. It was so bright that everyone could see it even through the thick thatches of the hut.

"Cover your ears quickly!" Fuxi ordered urgently.

Just after the ball of light appeared, piercing screams resounded. "Waah! Waah!"

After a while, the screams stopped.

"So, that's a Treacherous Being?" Eastern Emperor Taiyi asked as he pointed at the ball of light seen roaming outside.

When they looked through the thatches, they found that the ball of light had a rather irregular shape and that the piercing screams actually came from it.

"That's right. It seems that they have begun to move," the Snake Goddess replied with a nod.

While they were still conversing, another Treacherous Being appeared from the distance.

And like the first one, it also let out shrilling screams.

As time passed by, more and more Treacherous Beings appeared.

In the beginning, they were still able to bear the head-splitting howls, but as the Treacherous Beings grew larger in number, the howls seemed to be endless and it was as if their energies were being drained.

Soon, their faces contorted badly and turned blue as they became distressed.

"Is it going to continue for the whole night?" Zen asked in a low voice, holding his aching head.

The Snake Goddess smiled bitterly and said, "One thing is for sure, it's just the beginning. There is a division of labor among the Treacherous Beings.

Every night, they will gather together and howl desperately. These deafening screams could actually be heard even from faraway places."

The howls had been so terrifying. If ordinary people were on the receiving end, they would surely drive them crazy.

This was because it wasn't just a simple howl, but an aggressive spiritual attack.

"I don't think we can bear this for several hours. Is there something that we can do?" Yasamin asked with a livid face. Her heart was thumping so fast because of restlessness.

"Destroy your hearing," Fuxi blurted out of nowhere. "We can still use our spiritual senses to communicate with each other. We just need to repair our hearing tomorrow morning."

Fuxi's words made sense to everyone. Yasamin quickly raised her hands and stabbed her eardrums with her fingers.

Her hearing was instantly destroyed as a stream of blood came out from her ears. Immediately after, her face relaxed and a clear expression of relief was seen.

Without thinking twice, Eastern Emperor Taiyi, King Ieuan, the Wing King, and the three Eternal Realm Hunters also followed suit and stabbed their eardrums.

It would be pretty easy for them to restore their damaged hearing afterward, so there was no point in enduring a senseless struggle. It was more accurate to say that they "turned off" their hearing rather than "destroyed them".

"Zen, what about you? Can you still bear the howls?" The Snake Goddess asked as she took a glance at Zen.

"Yes, I'm fine," Zen replied.

"You don't have to be stubborn. The Treacherous Beings' howls go against nature. They can make you collapse. You have to destroy your hearing before it takes a greater toll on you," the Snake Goddess warned.

"Okay," Zen answered.

At this moment, the last of the Treacherous Beings walked past the hut and let out a sharp howl. After this, the village fell into a brief silence again.

Eastern Emperor Taiyi and the others had already destroyed their hearing, so they didn't have any reaction to the sudden change in the surroundings.

However, for Zen and the others that still had their normal hearing, the sudden tranquility didn't seem natural.

Unfortunately, the silence didn't last for long.

Through the thatches, they saw from a distance that the white balls of light were gathering again. In just a matter of seconds, the next wave of deafening howls resounded through the sky.

Previously, the Treacherous Beings howled in rapid succession, but this time, they howled in groups. The sharpness was the same as before, but the power they contained was much stronger.

"Woofâ€¦"

The Augury Dog barked in a low voice and looked at Fuxi with a pitiful face.

Fuxi then gently tapped the dog's ears with his fingers, and also damaged his hearing.

It was the turn of Fuxi and the Snake Goddess to "turn off" their hearing.

Before doing so, Fuxi turned to Zen again and said, "Why are you hesitating? Hurry up and just do it."

Although Zen's endurance was much stronger than the others, he still felt tortured as the howls grew louder and louder.

He decided to follow Fuxi and also stabbed his eardrums with his fingers.

As he pierced his eardrums, a brief rumbling sound reverberated in his head. Then, the entire world surrounding him became quiet. There wasn't a single sound to be heard.

However, just then, he felt a cool sensation hovering in his ears.

Then, he realized that his hearing had completely recovered.

This time, the ear-piercing howls sounded so much louder than before. It was as if the noise was drilling through his skull.

When Fuxi, the Snake Goddess, and the others saw Zen desperately holding his head with a facial expression of excruciating pain, they were shocked and confused.

"Zen, what's wrong?" the Snake Goddess asked through her spiritual sense.

"My hearing is restored," Zen answered as he endured the pain he was experiencing.

"What? How?" The Snake Goddess was bewildered at what just happened to him.

Then, she started to realize that it must have something to do with his bloodline.

'Don't tell meâ€¦ The bloodline restored his hearing?' the Snake Goddess thought as she narrowed her eyes.

"Waah! Waah!"

The Treacherous Beings outside once again let out a wave of high-pitched howls which seemed to be ten times louder than before.

The piercing screams started to mess up Zen's mind, so he stabbed his ears and destroyed his hearing. In an instant, he became deaf again.

Just when he thought that there was silence again, his hearing was restored at a faster rate this time.

The howls resounded in his ears again.

"Damn it! Again!"

Zen stabbed his ears again.

However, this time, his hearing was restored before he even felt the pain of stabbing himself in his ears.

When everyone saw him repeatedly stabbing his ears, they were confused and worried. They used their spiritual senses to ask the Snake Goddess about what happened. After knowing what happened, they were rendered speechless, and they looked at Zen with sympathy.

After stabbing his own ears for over a hundred times, Zen finally chose to give up and just let the howls resound in his ears.

Currently, the ancestry-level bloodline was still unable to replace him.

Otherwise, it wouldn't need such a troublesome method to make him suffer.

However, there must be other reasons for it to do so.

Zen gritted his teeth and sat with his legs crossed. He gathered his resolve and wore a serious face.

Since he couldn't avoid hearing the howls, he had no choice but to do his best to bear them.

Neither Fuxi nor the Snake Goddess knew how devastating the Treacherous Beings' howls could be. Every night, they would destroy their hearing before they experienced a much more intense level of the howls.

An hour hadn't even passed but the intense pain had already been unbearable for Zen. The entire night would last for twenty hours. That meant his suffering would be unimaginable.

While everyone was staring at Zen with a worried face, they still maintained sharp vigilance.

If the Treacherous Beings found out where they were hiding, it meant immediate death for them.

They also had to keep watch on Zen. If the moment came that he wasn't able to control himself and started wreaking havoc because of the pain, they would need to stop him at all costs.

Fortunately, Zen's pain and suffering only lasted for about four hours. As the painful expression on Zen's face gradually disappeared, it was replaced by a suspicious look.

He knew that there was something wrong going on. The howls had changed and turned into low chanting sounds.

Chapter 3991 Calling Fuxi had been observing Zen closely the whole time.

He was curious as to why Zen's pained expression gradually calmed down.

"Zen, have you sealed off your hearing?" he asked through his spiritual sense.

Zen was still carefully distinguishing the low chanting sounds. When he heard Fuxi's question, he shook his head and said, "No."

"It seems that you're not in pain anymoreâ€¦" At that point, Fuxi was even more surprised.

"The howls are gone. The Treacherous Beings you mentioned seem to be chanting something now," said Zen.

Fuxi arched his brows at Zen's words. "What are they chanting about?"

Before they entered the Whining Road, he and the Snake Goddess prepared quite well.

After all, they would die if they were not careful on their way to the Supreme Pure Realm.

When they hid in the thatched hut before, they also destroyed their hearing.

However, Fuxi brought out a mouse from his spirit beast bag every once in a while, so they knew what was going on outside.

The howls on the Whining Road were very powerful. Fuxi's mice also came from the Grand Pure Realm, and they were close relatives of the Terror Mice. Although they weren't rare creatures, they were by no means weak.

However, after the mouse was out for less than nine seconds, its eyes turned bloody red, then its head exploded as it struggled madly.

Generally speaking, the Whining Road had twelve hours of daytime and twenty hours of nighttime.

Fuxi released a mouse every two hours to test the situation.

According to his experiment, the howls lasted twenty hours until dawn.

It was not until daybreak when the mouse he had released returned unharmed, that he and the Snake Goddess dared to restore their hearing.

Based on the mice's reaction, the howls of the Treacherous Beings would last a whole night.

However, Zen just said that the howls had stopped, which contradicted his early conclusion. He didn't believe him at all.

Yet, Zen's reaction told him everything, as he didn't show any pain at all.

Did something happen to the Treacherous Beings on the Whining Road? Suddenly, an idea occurred to him. He gently touched his ears, as his palm glowed green. Then, his hearing returned to normal.

He had trusted Zen's reaction too much, but he forgot that Zen had a completely different type of life form after he had obtained a unique bloodline.

Just as he recovered his hearing, the ear-piercing howls immediately flooded his mind.

As a result, his eyes rolled back, and his body convulsed.

"Do you want to die?!" the Snake Goddess hissed madly.

She quickly reached out to him and pressed on his ears. After she shut off his hearing, he stopped twitching. He had fully fainted.

Then, she turned to look at Zen. "What did you do?" she asked in confusion.

He and Fuxi had communicated with each other through their spiritual senses just now, so the Snake Goddess naturally did not know what they talked about, nor did she know why Fuxi suddenly restored his hearing.

However, Zen was also confused. He said, "The Treacherous Beings have stopped wailing. Why did Master Fuxi still suffer?"

"Stopped wailing?" the Snake Goddess frowned. "Maybe you heard a different sound from us," she opined.

By that time, Fuxi woke up already. He released a spiritual sense that conveyed resentment. He glared at Zen and said, "You brat, do you want to kill me?"

Right now, the howls of the Treacherous Beings were quite intense. If it wasn't for the Snake Goddess's quick reaction, Fuxi's soul would've gotten seriously injured. Furthermore, exposure to the howls for five minutes was enough to kill him! "It's my fault, Master Fuxi," Zen apologized. "But what I hear are indeed chanting sounds, and the chants follow certain rules," he explained.

With that, he announced his words to the crowd in the thatched hut through his spiritual sense.

"Chants that follow some rules..."

"Do these Treacherous Beings have language?"

"You must have misheard it. Did the wails damage your ears?"

The Snake Goddess, Fuxi, and the three Eternal Realm Hunters all looked at him strangely.

No one knew about the origins of the Treacherous Beings. They just appeared occasionally in the Supreme Pure Realm.

It seemed that some kind of creature had created them from their resentment. As for why they existed or what they came here for, no one knew. The more they couldn't figure out the Treacherous Beings' origins, the more they became afraid of them.

"I did not mishear," Zen said and shook his head. "These regular chants seem to..."

As he spoke, his eyes suddenly glowed brightly, then he exclaimed, "It appears that they are reciting Sanskrit words!"

The voices uttered the chants in a rhythm. Although their tone was flat and was nothing like singing, it was quite similar to reading Sanskrit words.

Back then, when he was with the bald giant by the name of Pompeo, his voice was like singing, and it was also rhythmic.

It turned out that the Treacherous Beings were not wailing, but communicating through the incomprehensible Sanskrit words! "Sanskrit words?"

Everyone looked at each other, confused.

"Ha-ha! Forget about whether the Treacherous Beings know Sanskrit or not, or if the wails are a way of their communication with Sanskrit words. Even if it is, you still can't understand it," Pearson said and waved his hand.

There was no way for them to confirm such speculations if they couldn't understand the language used. Thus, Pearson thought that what Zen said was nonsense.

"Not necessarily," the Snake Goddess said with a smile. "He can understand it."

Pearson's, Thurston's, and Sawyer's eyes widened in shock. They thought that the Snake Goddess must be kidding! The Eternal Realm Hunters wandered in the Three Purities Stage all year round, and they also knew a lot about Sanskrit words.

It was still possible to decipher Sanskrit words that were on paper or engraved on something, but not for "Sanskrit words" in chants.

That kind of language contained too much meaning, and it was too complicated.

Furthermore, the creatures in the chaos had innate limitations. Letting them decipher Sanskrit words was equivalent to making the dumb speak and the blind paint. It was beyond their abilities.

Even Eastern Emperor Taiyi and Yasamin also cast Zen strange looks. Then again, they did not know much about what happened on the Other Shore after they got trapped, so they did not know that Zen had such a skill.

"I'm not sure if I can understand, but I can try," said Zen.

What if perhaps the Treacherous Beings did not talk in Sanskrit? If so, the Heavenly Obsession Civilization naturally couldn't decipher them.

Still, he began to communicate with the Heavenly Obsession Civilization.

However, he didn't dare let the Heavenly Obsession Civilization listen directly to the wails. Instead, he transmitted the sound he heard into his inner world.

Once the Civilization Artifact of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization was ready, it began to decipher the chants.

At the same time, the core of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization on the upper ice field of the Blooming Jade Stage began to operate like mad.

This time, it took longer to decipher the words. After quite a while, a voice came out from the Civilization Artifact.

"They are indeed speaking Sanskrit," it stated. "Then what are they talking about?" Zen asked hurriedly.

"Most of the sounds are meaningless. Perhaps they are scriptures used in a kind of ceremony, and they recite them over and over again," answered the Civilization Artifact.

"Some scriptures..." In all honesty, he was a little disappointed.

Just then, the Civilization Artifact added, "In addition to those meaningless scriptures, there is also a sentence within them."

He immediately perked up upon hearing those words. "What is it?" he asked again.

"They have been calling out 'come back quickly, ' as if one of them went missing. They continually repeat the words so the missing would return,"

the Civilization Artifact said.

Chapter 3992 Revive Come back quickly...

Since the Heavenly Obsession Civilization heard this sentence from the wails of the Treacherous Beings, it meant that they were indeed using Sanskrit.

But who were they calling for? "How is it going? Do you understand what they are talking about?" the Snake Goddess asked while Zen was in deep concentration.

"I can't understand most of the sounds. They seem to be some kind of scripture," Zen paused, realizing everyone was looking at him.

Of all the warriors present, only the Wing King, Fuxi, and the Snake Goddess believed that Zen could understand Sanskrit words.

Fuxi and the Snake Goddess knew what happened in the Blooming Jade Stage; and since the Wing King and a Civilization Artifact in Zen's body were bound together, he was also aware of it.

Others remained skeptical, including Eastern Emperor Taiyi. He and Yasamin had just been rescued and did not have enough time to know about the current situation.

"Are they reciting only scriptures?" Fuxi asked.

"In addition to the scriptures, they also seem to be calling for a companion to return," Zen said admittedly.

"Really? Are you sure you didn't mishear?" Pearson chuckled beside him.

The Eternal Realm Hunters didn't believe Zen's words at all. Looking at his seemingly serious expression, they assumed that Zen was talking nonsense.

Zen dismissed Pearson's sarcastic words. He shook his head and said, "No, I'm sure about what I heard."

The core of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization didn't decipher without any basis.

There were only two results of the deciphering: either it was unable to decipher, or it deciphered every word accurately.

Since the core of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization had deciphered it, the information should be correct.

"You are so confident," Thurston said as his eyes glimmered.

"That's it. They indeed lost one companion, so they keep calling for their companion to return," the Snake Goddess suddenly concluded.

Pearson questioned, "You don't know much about the Treacherous Beings, and you just passed the Whining Road by luck. How could you be so certain?"

Pearson could tell that Fuxi and the Snake Goddess were inexperienced in dealing with the Treacherous Beings. They had just hidden in the thatched hut in the past and snuck away after three days when the Treacherous Beings disappeared.

In comparison, Pearson had personally witnessed the Treacherous Beings in the Supreme Pure Realm. He believed that he understood the Treacherous Beings better than everyone.

The Snake Goddess smiled slightly, reading between the lines of his words.

"There are two hundred thatched huts here. In the past, every thatched hut had a Treacherous Being inside, totaling two hundred Treacherous Beings.

Now, there are only one hundred and ninety-nine of them. That means one is missing, and a thatched hut is vacant,"

she said as she pointed to the ground, referring to where they were all staying. It was the vacant thatched hut.

The reason why the Whining Road had been difficult to pass was that Treacherous Beings were something no one could resist.

Many Eternal Realm warriors and nonhuman creatures chose to walk this path; but no matter the number, they all had been annihilated.

This made the Whining Road notorious for its cruelty...

Now, there was a Treacherous Being missing from the Whining Roadâ€“a thatched hut had become empty. They had used this loophole to pass through the Whining Road.

Hearing the Snake Goddess' explanation, Pearson immediately comprehended. He looked at Zen with enlightenment.

Zen actually could understand Sanskrit words...

"Just as Zen said, they are calling for their companion to return. If that Treacherous Being returns, wouldn't we be in trouble?" King Ieuan suddenly asked.

"It had not been back for so many years. What are the odds that it would come back today?" Fuxi answered, rolling his eyes at it.

The Snake Goddess and Fuxi previously had this concern. The two of them were nervous when they couldn't find the empty thatched hut, but now there was no need to worry.

For twenty hours, everyone still had their hearing completely shut. They couldn't hear anything while Zen, on the other hand, continued to listen attentively to the chants.

The core of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization had been working as well, trying its best to decipher even a little information for Zen.

However, these Treacherous Beings behaved stubbornly...

For nearly twenty hours, they had been reciting the scriptures with only a little communication between them.

Dawn came at the end of the last hour. A faint light peeped from outside the thatched hut.

The strange Treacherous Beings all returned inside of their own thatched hut. They started to communicate while Zen successfully decoded the communication part by part.

A Treacherous Being started walking towards Zen and his group's thatched hut. The Treacherous Being's footsteps approached, with everyone becoming more anxious as they felt it getting closer and closer.

"What should we do?" King Ieuan panicked.

The Snake Goddess made a gesture, warning it not to use spiritual sense to communicate with others in case they would be discovered by the Treacherous Beings.

She walked carefully to the edge of the thatched hut. When the Treacherous Being was about to lift the edge, the Snake Goddess grabbed it, forcing it to shut. The Treacherous Being failed to open it, eventually giving up after several tries.

The Treacherous Being turned around to look for another thatched hut instead. It walked further from them, putting everyone's heart at ease. They sighed in relief.

Soon, the sky revealed its full brightness. The Snake Goddess told everyone to recover their hearing and opened the thatched hut.

Everyone walked out the thatched hut one by one. Twenty hours inside such a small space had left them in discomfort. They lifted their arms and bent their bodies to stretch.

"Staying on this road for three days and directly entering the Supreme Pure Realm is the easiest thing we've done in history," Pearson said with confidence.

"I remember the first time we entered the Supreme Pure Realm, half of us died..." Thurston sentimentally recalled. The Eternal Realm Hunters were all elites, but even they had to pay a huge price in going to the Supreme Pure Realm.

While everyone was breathing and enjoying the fresh air, the Snake Goddess found that Zen's face was a little gloomy. "Zen, what's wrong?"

Everyone turned their glances, once again focusing on him.

After hesitating for a moment, Zen asked, "Is it really impossible to kill the Treacherous Beings?"

"Yes, it's impossible to kill them," Pearson quickly answered. "Even if they get killed, they will still come back to life. They can't disappear from the world."

The Treacherous Beings were the real indestructible existences in the Three Purities Stage.

"What exactly did you hear again?" the Snake Goddess asked.

"The Treacherous Beings exchanged a few words before they went into the thatched huts. Their companion is trapped outside the Whining Road, which seems to be the Supreme Pure Realm," Zen replied.

"It might have been trapped there for many years." Fuxi nodded.

"But the trapped Treacherous Being has been killed recently. They are trying to find a way to revive it, and they would do it tonight..." Zen continued.

Everyone fell silent upon hearing his statement.

The Snake Goddess stared at Zen nervously. "Are you sure?"

"I'm afraid so," Zen agreed.

King Ieuan interrupted, "If that Treacherous Being comes back to life, doesn't that mean there won't be any vacant thatched hut?"

The Snake Goddess and Fuxi shared a dull aura, their faces darkening in fear.

One more Treacherous Being meant that they would lose their hiding place.

If the Treacherous Beings discovered them, they would definitely be attacked. Everyone could die! "Do we still have a chance to retreat?" Eastern Emperor Taiyi asked as his face turned into a frown.

"If we quit the Whining Road before the duration of three days ends, we will not be able to enter the Supreme Pure Realm nor could we return to the Grand Pure Realm. We will only be lost in the plain where we can never turn back," the Snake Goddess said.

"What should we do now?" Yasamin asked, her face flooded with worry.

The Snake Goddess glanced at the thatched huts. "The only way now is to kill another Treacherous Being," she firmly declared.

Chapter 3993 A Hard Choice Zen and his companions were in great trouble at that point. If the Treacherous Being came back to life and couldn't find its thatched hut, it would hunt them down.

It was most likely that two hundred Treacherous Beings would probably come for them.

Furthermore, Treacherous Beings' strengths only gave them a slim chance of survival.

Had it been one Treacherous Being, perhaps they might still make it.

The Snake Goddess's idea might work.

"Are you sure you want to fight a Treacherous Being?" Pearson sniffed. "Or what? Should we surrender to them instead?" Fuxi asked darkly. "I did not mean to look down on you," Pearson said indifferently. "There was once a race called the Primal Tiger race, in the Grand Pure Realm.

They were so powerful that even the Element Spirit Civilization never dared to provoke them. We were lucky enough to befriend themâ€¦" he continued.

Although the Eternal Realm Hunters usually traveled alone, they did have some friends in the Three Purities Stage.

For instance, the Primal Tiger race was on friendly terms with the Eternal Realm Hunters.

In the past, when dozens of members of the Primal Tiger race fell into a poisonous well, it was the Eternal Realm Hunters who had saved them.

Due to immense gratitude, the Primal Tiger race had promised to protect the Eternal Realm Hunters forever.

After that, the Eternal Realm Hunters turned to the Primal Tiger race whenever they were in peril. That was how they escaped their end several times.

However, a single Treacherous Being slaughtered such a strong race that not even the Element Spirit Civilization dared to instigate! Back then, the Eternal Realm Hunters were also in the tribe of the Primal Tiger race. They didn't take the Treacherous Being seriously at first since they thought that the mighty Primal Tiger race would deal with it.

Even when the Eye Spirit had personally visited the Primal Tiger race to ask for the Eternal Realm Hunters, they just drove him away. Therefore, who else in the Three Purities Stage posed any threat to them? Soon enough, the Eternal Realm Hunters found that they were very wrong.

Simply put, the Treacherous Being's power was far beyond their imagination.

At that time, the Eternal Realm Hunters had only gotten a glimpse of the Treacherous Being. It was a continually changing spirit.

After the Treacherous Being broke into the tribe, it immediately exploded and unleashed blood-red flames that had spread in all directions.

As a result, the vast majority of the Primal Tiger race did not have a chance to escape at all, and the red flames swallowed them.

The Eternal Realm Hunters stayed on the edge of the tribe's territory. When they saw the spread of red flames, they quickly fled into the distance â€” but the red flames still slaughtered three of them.

Even though one of the victims had only barely brushed against the flames, he seemed to have suffered the worst curse in the world. His body crumpled, and his soul turned grey. He faded away each passing day. The others infused their life energies into him but to no avail. In the end, he had died miserably after several months of struggle and torture.

From then on, the Eternal Realm Hunters finally understood the real power of the Treacherous Beings.

After Pearson finished his story, Eastern Emperor Taiyi, Yasamin, King Ieuan, the Snake Goddess, and even Fuxi, all shared dark looks.

The Snake Goddess and Fuxi knew that the Treacherous Beings were horrible creatures, but this was beyond their expectations.

"So what should we do? Do we have no chance of survival at all?" asked Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

If the Treacherous Beings were surely that powerful, they could not fight back.

"I don't think all of them are as strong as the one in the story.

We may still have a way to deal with them," Zen suddenly said. "What made you think that?" Eastern Emperor Taiyi asked.

"Someone must have used a special method to drive that Treacherous Being off and sent it to the Supreme Pure Realm," Zen said as he pointed at the thatched huts in the distance.

It was clear that a Treacherous Being in the Whining Road would not leave the place for no reason. Thus, someone must have found a way to lure it to the Supreme Pure Realm. Since someone had managed to do that, they could also deal with a Treacherous Being if they did find a way.

"I agree. Someone must have driven that Treacherous Being away. If we try, maybe we'll also have a chance," the Snake Goddess said.

Then, Thurston asked, "Zen, are you sure that Treacherous Being will come back to life tonight?"

Zen shook his head. "I'm not completely sure about that. I heard the other Treacherous Beings discuss that they would bring it back to life tonight, but it does not mean that they'll manage to do so," he answered.

Upon hearing his explanation, everyone became hesitant.

It seemed that the chances of the Treacherous Being's rebirth were not high, but once it came back to life, death and destruction would follow.

On the other hand, if they took the initiative to kill another Treacherous Being first, it was not an easy feat at all. They remained stuck in a dilemma.

At that moment, the Wing King, who usually did not speak much, abruptly said, "Don't pin your hopes on others. Losing the initiative is equivalent to waiting passively to be killed!"

The Regal Jade Civilization had placed their hopes on the Nihility race in the past, as they thought that the enemies would pull their punches. In the end, the Regal Jade Civilization had met a tragic end.

"You're right. Once the night falls, we'll have no more chances to fight back," Fuxi said with a nod.

Meanwhile, King Ieuan looked at Thurston and Sawyer, then said, "You can summon the powerful Black Sun, right? If you can pull a Treacherous Being into the Black Sun, then killing it won't be that hard, right?"

It was true that the Black Sun had severe limitations, but it was useful when it came to individual enemies.

"Well, we can try," Thurston agreed. In fact, he already thought of that idea, and that was why he had asked Zen the question.

"Each Treacherous Being has a different level of strength. We still have enough time. We need to find out the easiest opponent," Pearson stated.

Fortunately, daytime in the Whining Road was twelve hours long, so they had sufficient time to prepare before nightfall.

Of course, the task of choosing their opponent fell on the Augury Dog, who was the most sensitive to powers.

He could sense the level of threat of each enemy, which was associated with their strength.

A few leaves gently rustled on the ground as the Augury Dog ran past each of the thatched huts and sniffed them one by one. Every time he passed by a thatched hut, his eyes became filled with fear. However, he went to the next thatched hut without hesitation.

Not long after, he had examined over one hundred thatched huts. When only three huts remained, the Augury Dog stopped before one of the huts and said in a low voice, "This one. This one is the weakest among them all."

The thatched hut he referred to was isolated from the rest.

Still, it emanated a threatening aura.

Then again, it was indeed a little weaker compared to the other Treacherous Beings.

"Get ready," Fuxi said to the three Eternal Realm Hunters.

The three Eternal Realm Hunters had decided their divisions of labor.

Pearson was responsible for subduing the Treacherous Being, while Thurston and Sawyer would pull it into the Black Sun.

If everything went well, the whole ordeal would only take them a short while.

Now, the others retreated to a safe distance and formed a circle to deal with emergencies.

Finally, they shut off their hearing, then Thurston and Sawyer summoned the Black Sun.

At that point, Pearson turned into a spider web and blocked the front of the thatched hut. "Who will open the thatched hut for us?" Sawyer asked.

His question met silence. Everyone looked reluctant to do the dangerous task.

"I'll do it," Zen said in a resolute voice.

He walked straight to the thatched hut, grabbed a corner of the flap, and slowly lifted it.

The whole village in the vast, white mist was unusually quiet, to the point that everyone heard their heartbeats clearly.

When Zen had lifted more than half of the flap, they all saw a strange thing that lay on the ground.

It looked like a mass of white liquid, but it had limbs and a head.

It also had two black hollows on its head. Everyone felt afraid when they looked into the holes.

"So this is a Treacherous Being..."

"Is it asleep?"

"Its aura feels depressing..."

Without the thatched hut as a barrier, they were now face to face with the Treacherous Being. The air around it felt so uncomfortable, and it overwhelmed them even more.

It appeared that the Treacherous Being was the nemesis of all living beings.

They couldn't help but feel instinctively fearful in front of it.

Zen took a few steps back and nodded at the Eternal Realm Hunters, which signaled them to get started.

Chapter 3994 Possessed By The Treacherous Being The Treacherous Being was not on-guard at all and seemed to have fallen asleep.

Very few people had ever dared to venture into the Whining Road since ancient times. Not many were brave enough to challenge the Treacherous Beings after all.

Nobody ever came through here, thus the Treacherous Beings did not see the need to be so vigilant.

"Hiss, hiss, hiss..."

One by one, long, thin threads crept up towards the Treacherous Being.

Extremely thin to the point of weightlessness, these spider threads felt no more than specks of dust upon the body of the Treacherous Being.

Soon enough, these threads covered the creature in its entirety. Every single square inch was tightly wrapped by the spider threads! Swoosh...

The Black Sun in front of Thurston and Sawyer began to spin just as a strong attraction force burst forth from it.

As this strong attraction force came out, it headed straight towards the Treacherous Being and dragged it directly out of the thatched hut.

Its body was soft, liquid, and had the consistency of water. It had since lost its shape and had turned into something that resembled a mass of sticky glue.

"Whoosh!"

With no struggle on the part of the Treacherous Being, it was quickly and flawlessly sucked into the Black Sun.

It was only then that Thurston and Sawyer separated and the Black Sun promptly disappeared.

If one thought about it, it was actually quite amazing. A horrible Treacherous Being was dealt with in such a short amount of time and with no sort of violent struggle whatsoever.

Eastern Emperor Taiyi had to voice out his question through spiritual sense.

"Has the Treacherous Being been sucked in?"

Yasamin nodded. "I suppose."

The Wing King then took his chance to slowly withdraw his wings.

An open space was necessary to deal with a Treacherous Being. If it ever let out a howl to call out its companions, the Wing King would use the space to block off any sound, if it could block it at all.

With their purpose served, the spider threads retreated and reformed into Pearson's body.

"You two should separate further," he ordered Sawyer and Thurston. The Black Sun had never failed them until Zen, of course.

Even if the Treacherous Being was sucked into the Black Sun, it was best to be careful.

What if it turned out that the Treacherous Being shared Zen's ability? What if like the young man, it could also forcibly gather the separated Black Sun? If that was the case, then things would be very bad for all of them.

Sawyer and Thurston did as Pearson ordered and walked further in the opposite direction of each other.

However, Sawyer had only taken a few steps when a white mass suddenly emerged from his back.

It was the sticky body of the Treacherous Being! Pearson was quick to point out this horrifying mass. "Sawyer!" he roared in warning. In a fit of desperation, he had forgotten that everyone had destroyed their hearing and only Zen heard what he said.

Sawyer had no idea what was currently on his back and of the warnings Pearson yelled at him.

The white mass of goo gradually bulged and extended its body on top of Sawyer's head. Then two, hollow eyes appeared.

There was no denying that the Treacherous Being had used some kind of technique to escape the Black Sun before it closed.

"Up there! Above your head!" the Snake Goddess warned Sawyer through spiritual sense. Her words were firm but unlike Pearson; she knew how to use her head.

Panic in their current situation was never a good thing.

When Sawyer raised his head, he immediately paled.

How could this be? This thing had attached itself onto his back! The Treacherous Being was a mass of goo and looked like a slug as it crawled on Sawyer's back. Anyone would get goose bumps just imagining it. When Sawyer turned his head, the Treacherous Being took the chance and planted itself on his face! Swish! Swish! Swish...

The orifices on Sawyer's face were enough for the Treacherous Being to enter his body.

In the blink of an eye, the mass of goo was gone and had completely entered Sawyer! "Sawyer, no!" Thurston screamed. A sudden rage erupted from deep inside him when he saw what happened.

However, along with the anger came fear.

Everything happened so fast. There was no time to react, much less help Sawyer.

With the Treacherous Being now inside him, Sawyer's pupils suddenly rolled back and he stood completely still.

The people around him immediately stepped back, eager to keep their distance.

To everyone's horror, Sawyer turned towards Zen and opened his mouth. He was going to start howling! "Buzz!"

There was a flash of green light as the Wing King spread his wings and formed a protective dome above all of them.

Fuxi and the Snake Goddess could only look up in desperate hopes that Sawyer's howls wouldn't wake up the other Treacherous Beings.

Everyone waited with bated breath to see if the protective dome would do its job.

"It works!" they all exclaimed when they saw the thatched huts remain quiet.

To say that they were relieved would be an understatement.

They couldn't be too sure if the space the Wing King conjured completely blocked Sawyer's howls but it proved to be enough since none of the other Treacherous Beings stirred from their slumber.

However, they still had a problem.

"Zen, can you understand what it's saying?" the Snake Goddess asked him through spiritual sense as the Treacherous Being continued to howl.

"It is being deciphered," he replied.

Since the Black Sun's space failed to trap this Treacherous Being, then this situation had now truly become extremely troublesome.

"Should we kill it?" Fuxi asked. Thurston was quick to shake his head.

"No! Of course not!" he exclaimed.

Sawyer was his brother and there was no way he would be willing to kill him. Thurston would rather kill himself than hurt his brother.

"What should we do then?" Fuxi asked. This situation wasn't exactly ideal.

A Treacherous Being's strength was unfathomable and even if the warriors had an advantage, victory remained slippery.

If they waited until the Treacherous Being began to attack them, they would be forced into a passive state.

"I don't care what we do but anyone who hurts my brother will be my enemy," Thurston declared as he shot Fuxi a cold glare. It was obvious that keeping his brother safe and sound was non-negotiable.

"Calm down Thurston. You must remember, that person is no longer Sawyer!" Pearson reminded him.

There were so many monsters in the Three Purities Stage that had the ability of possession.

The Soul-killing Flame for instance was one of these creatures. It existed in the Grand Pure Realm and could possess one's body if a warrior was not too careful. The Soul Leech in the Blood Swamp of the Supreme Pure Realm was another example.

A warrior could already be considered dead the moment these creatures possessed their body.

Since the Treacherous Being was infinitely more terrifying than those things then how could they ever hope for Sawyer's survival?! He was no more than a corpse now! Thurston shook his head in denial.

"But...But..." he stammered and watched as his brother, who had previously been content with howling, suddenly rushed towards Zen.

"We need to act now!" Fuxi declared.

Without any hesitation, he stretched out his hand and pressed it onto the ground.

A mark of Eight Diagrams promptly appeared on top of Sawyer's head.

In his determination to take down Sawyer, Fuxi exerted his full strength onto this attack.

Just as Fuxi's attack came down upon the young man, Sawyer suddenly pointed up and touched the mark of Eight Diagrams. To everyone's surprise, it shattered with a loud bang! The attack, backed by Fuxi's full strength, was broken by Sawyer so casually.

Swish! Swish! Swish...

The Snake Goddess also went on the offensive and stretched out her shadow's densely-packed tentacles to wrap around Sawyer.

Meanwhile, King Ieuan, Eastern Emperor Taiyi, and Yasamin got busy with using their own unique skills.

Underneath this green space, the collection of powerful energy and the pressure it released was terrifying. Any ordinary creature would tremble in fear.

Unfortunately, the thing that possessed Sawyer was far from ordinary. The Treacherous Being had an incredible ability that dissipated any sort of energy sent to harm it.

When Zen saw Sawyer rush towards him, his eyes immediately flashed with determination. Instead of a retreat, he decided to face his opponent head-on.

Eager to take on the offensive, Zen lowered his body and threw a solid punch towards Sawyer's head! "Da!"

Since his body had been transformed by the ancestry-level bloodline, it was a given that the power of his punch would be extremely terrifying.

However, instead of the devastating results Zen expected, Sawyer merely stretched out his finger and pointed it to his fist.

The moment their hands touched, Zen's power completely dissipated.

His pupils widened and he immediately jumped back in retreat.

"What the...? No. Retreat! Retreat!"

Unfortunately, that was no longer an option. Sawyer was fast and immediately grabbed hold of Zen's fist. He didn't seem to exert that much strength but Zen found himself unable to break free of his hold.

"Rumble, rumble, rumble..."

At that moment, a stream of white goo emerged from the orifices of Sawyer's face. It was the Treacherous Being's body! Soon enough, Zen found himself face to face with the Treacherous Being's hollow eyes and its strange smile. It looked at him up and down before suddenly jumping onto his face and into his body the same way it entered Sawyer.

Chapter 3995 The Soul Catching Lamp Thud! Sawyer's unconscious body fell to the ground.

At the same time, Zen lowered his head and stood still. Previously, when Sawyer was being possessed by the Treacherous Being, he wasn't able to move either. This time, it seemed that it was trying to invade Zen's body.

"Brother!" Thurston quickly approached Sawyer's body.

He carefully carried Sawyer to one corner to look at his condition.

The others didn't pay much attention to Sawyer right now, for they were all focused on Zen.

Everyone knew how important Zen was. If the Treacherous Being successfully invaded his body, there might be dire consequences.

"What should we do now?" Eastern Emperor Taiyi asked in a panic.

"We have to somehow find a way to drive the Treacherous Being out of his body!" King Ieuan said anxiously, also not knowing what exactly was needed to be done.

Then, the Snake Goddess's eyes narrowed as she walked towards Zen. She stretched out her hand, and a pink flower lamp immediately materialized.

"The Soul Catching Lamp!"

Everyone's eyes lit up as they saw the lamp emerge from the Snake Goddess's hand.

The flower contained in the Soul Catching Lamp could forcefully drive the soul out of one's body.

Even if that person had reached the Holy Soul Realm, he would still find it difficult to resist its power.

However, despite its power, its use was quite limited. This was because the lamp needed to be close to the target in order to be effective.

Because of this, it had never been used in battles.

But now that Zen's body was still motionless, the Soul Catching Lamp came in handy.

The only problem was that they weren't sure if the Treacherous Being was a kind of soul or not. If it wasn't, then the lamp would also be useless.

The Snake Goddess didn't have much time to think about it, so she just risked it.

Soon after, the pink flower in the lamp began to glow. Wisps of pink smoke started floating out from it.

Whoosh! The Snake Goddess forcefully blew the smoke.

The pink smoke quickly rushed towards Zen's face and entered into his eyes, ears, mouth, and nose.

Then, the Snake Goddess monitored the movements of the Soul Catching Lamp.

In just a matter of seconds, the pink light in the lamp grew brighter and brighter as the flower started blooming.

However, as the flower reached its full bloom, the light suddenly dimmed, and the petals began to wither rapidly.

With a flash in the Snake Goddess's eyes, she yelled, "Now!"

She started grabbing the Soul Catching Lamp and pulled it hard.

She felt that the smoke inside Zen's body latched onto something, so she was trying to pull it out from him.

Whoosh! Whoosh! Soon, wisps of pink smoke came out from Zen's eyes, ears, mouth, and nose.

Everyone was expecting that the Treacherous Being would be pulled out along with the pink smoke.

However, their faces twitched the moment they saw that there was nothing but the smoke.

The Snake Goddess was the most disappointed of all. She knew that she felt something earlier, so she was also surprised that nothing came out.

Whoosh! Unwilling to give up, the Snake Goddess once again blew the smoke into Zen's face.

Right now, everyone depended on her, so she couldn't fail them.

However, before the Snake Goddess could pull the smoke out again, Zen suddenly opened his eyes.

Everyone was shocked to see that the pupils in his eyes had disappeared.

His eyes only revealed the white parts, and it seemed that he was no longer in control of his body.

Then, in a split-second, the previously motionless body of Zen quickly rushed towards the Snake Goddess.

Crash! Zen threw a punch at the Snake Goddess.

The Snake Goddess was totally caught off guard. At such a close distance, she wasn't able to dodge Zen's sudden strike.

Although it was just an ordinary punch, the force it contained was still extremely terrifying.

The Snake Goddess instantly flew backward and was thrown far off to the point that she hit the circular space wall created by the Wing King.

Meanwhile, Zen opened his mouth and did the same thing as Sawyer did earlier. He was howling.

Then, he turned around and threw a punch at the green space wall.

Crash! The space wall instantly broke into pieces.

Whoosh! He then strode towards the exit of the village.

"What's going on? What's he going to do?"

"The Treacherous Being doesn't look like it would wake up its companions."

"Then, is it just going to leave this place?"

Everyone had a lot of questions in mind.

They also wanted to chase after Zen, but his speed was just too fast.

Moreover, they wouldn't be able to do anything with the Treacherous Being's strength even if they caught up with Zen.

Previously, when the Treacherous Being had possessed Sawyer's body, it had easily resisted the theurgies of the Eternal Realm warriors. Now that it possessed Zen's body, it was more likely that its strength would also be stronger.

In just a few seconds, Zen had already rushed out of the fences of the Whining Road and disappeared through the vast white mist.

King Ieuan, Eastern Emperor Taiyi, and the others just stood there as they watched Zen's figure vanish into the mist.

They were left dumbfounded at everything that just happened.

"But today is not the third day. Now that he just went out like this on his own, would he be lost on the plain?" King Ieuan couldn't help but ask anxiously.

At the same time, Fuxi was busy helping the Snake Goddess heal her wounds. He looked back and said flatly, "Theoretically, yes. However, there may be an exception."

After all, they all knew that the Whining Road belonged to the Treacherous Beings. Since it possessed Zen's body, then perhaps it wouldn't be lost.

But there were bigger problems to be considered, like Zen's survival.

Could he still survive after being possessed by it? The Snake Goddess was badly injured. But despite her condition, she hadn't stopped thinking of a way to save Zen. However, it seemed like she was also running out of ideas as her face showed an expression of hopelessness.

Eventually, everyone had stopped talking and the atmosphere became even gloomier. At this moment, the silence was broken when they heard someone cough.

"Ahem! W-what happened to me?"

While everyone was getting depressed, Sawyer suddenly woke up in Thurston's arms.

"Brother, you've come to!" Thurston was overjoyed. He was actually thinking if Sawyer was even going to wake up after being possessed by the Treacherous Being.

Everyone's attention focused on Sawyer. As he tried to recall what happened earlier, his face darkened. He started touching his face and his body but found out that he wasn't hurt.

"Brother, you're fine now. The Treacherous Being has come out of your body," Thurston explained in a soft voice.

All of them thought of the possibility that Sawyer might die. But it turned out that as the Treacherous Being left his body, it also left his body and soul intact.

"This is actually good news!"

"He's fine after being possessed by the Treacherous Being. That means that Zen could also survive!"

"That's right. At least there is still a chance."

As they saw that Sawyer was in good condition, everyone seemed to get a hold of a glimmer of hope.

"I'm connected to the Civilization Artifact of the Regal Jade Civilization, so I can sense his location. After we leave the Whining Road, we could go look for him," the Wing King suggested.

"That's good to know then," Fuxi said as he nodded his head.

Just earlier, they were almost about to give up. But now that they knew that there was slight hope of finding Zen, they decided to give their all for this slim chance.

Now, one more Treacherous Being had left the Whining Road. Even if a Treacherous Being really revived at night, there would still be an empty thatched hut here.

After several hours, the sky started to dim again.

The Whining Road was enveloped in darkness once more.

Thanks to Fuxi's treatment, most of the injuries of the Snake Goddess had already been healed.

Then, everyone stabbed their ears again as they went into hiding inside the small hut.

Through the thatches, they saw the Treacherous Beings flickering in bright white lights.

The Snake Goddess's eyes flashed as she concentrated on counting the Treacherous Beings roaming outside.

She counted a few times just to make sure. The result was still the same, and there were a total of one hundred and ninety-eight of them. It meant that two were missing.

The first one did not revive, and the other one was the one that possessed Zen's body.

Then, the night passed. As dawn drew near, all of the Treacherous Beings returned to the thatched huts.

They confirmed that one of the missing Treacherous Beings did not come back to life last night.

All of their faces seemed to be filled with regret.

They thought that making the move was a complete mistake.

However, no one knew what the result might be, so they needed to give it a try.

After that night, there was only one remaining.

Then, they could leave the following morning and enter the Supreme Pure Realm.

Chapter 3996 The Blood Swamp For the first time in their lives, Eastern Emperor Taiyi, Yasamin, King Ieuan, and the Wing King could finally set foot in the Supreme Pure Realm.

This was a momentous achievement for all of them.

This was a huge deal especially for the Wing King. Because no matter how powerful he was, he had never entered the Supreme Pure Realm yet.

Because this was their first time there, it would make sense for them to be full of expectations. They were supposed to enjoy and celebrate this wonderful accomplishment.

However, Zen had been missing for quite a while now. So instead of being excited, everyone's heart was heavy. This unfortunate occurrence had really dampened their spirits.

They discussed at length Zen's possible current whereabouts after he left the Whining Road. For the entire day, they only talked about where he could be and how they could possibly find him.

They were well-aware that talking about it while they were in the village would yield nothing. Still, it was obvious that Zen was extremely important to them.

Deep within the hearts of Fuxi and the Snake Goddess, they knew that Zen was the key to the completion of the Finale Way. He was their only hope.

Even if it would cost them their lives, they definitely would not hesitate to save him.

Twelve hours had passed by so quickly. Before they knew it, darkness had fallen once more.

It was nighttime on the Whining Road again. Before long, they heard familiar noises in the distance.

The Treacherous Beings were howling again. This had been happening for the past two nights already. They would appear as soon as the darkness had settled in.

So far, she had counted one hundred ninety-eight of them.

However, she suddenly discovered that some Treacherous Beings formed a strange shape on the Whining Road four hours later.

She kept observing them and realized they were gathering within an area and were making a circle.

All of a sudden, a strange and dazzling white light appeared at the center of the circle.

The Treacherous Beings as well as the white light were blinding. It was almost as if there was a sun shining at night.

The bright light illuminated the entire area so much that the people inside the thick thatched hut were able to see them clearly.

"What is that white light? Where is it coming from?"

"Look! It is getting bigger and bigger."

As the group watched this scene unfold right before their eyes, they noticed a change in the white light. Seeing this, they instantly had a guess as to what it was.

As the expanding white light began taking shape, it seemed clear to everyone what was really happening.

That specific Treacherous Being was being revived.

It became clear that Zen made the right decision.

If they had made the other choice earlier, they could still spend the second night safely, but it would not be the case this night.

The third night would be riddled with danger. They were quite sure about this.

It was sure as day that the Treacherous Beings would be able to find out they had occupied a thatched hut and attack them.

It would be impossible to hold off and stand against the Treacherous Beings by themselves.

She would've had gladly traded her life if it meant ensuring Zen's safety.

She would do this in a heartbeat not only for the completion of the Finale Way, but also for Dorothy's sake.

Everyone had seemed downcast ever since Zen's disappearance. They couldn't help but sigh and wish they could have done something.

Meanwhile, the Wing King kept observing the scene in the dark. All of a sudden, he spoke using his spiritual sense, "These Treacherous Beings don't seem like they have any sort of intelligence."

His statement was met with looks of utter confusion from everyone in their group. They couldn't quite figure out how or why he came to this conclusion.

They knew that Zen had already deciphered the conversations of the Treacherous Beings before.

Obviously, this meant that they had their own thoughts.

In addition to that, they were even able to resurrect their fallen companions.

How could they not possess any intelligence? "What makes you say that?" The Snake Goddess walked towards the Wing King and asked. Her face was full of curiosity.

"Well, it seems like they don't know that one of them is missing yet,"

replied the Wing King. "And whenever they aren't able to enter a thatched hut, they won't even try to force their way in to take a look. Instead, they will just move onto the next one. That way of doing things kind of strikes me as very mechanical," he added.

If the Treacherous Beings gathered into a group, they would have noticed that one of them was missing and would set out to find their companion.

Before the Wing King mentioned this, no one felt like there was anything wrong about them. But now that they thought about it, they realized how truly strange it was.

"Well, that's true." Fuxi nodded slowly with a frown on his face. He was trying to recall what happened for the past two nights. "Whenever the Treacherous Beings came, I just propped the thatches up and they would just leave. No one ever tried to enter and check."

The Snake Goddess tilted her head and was lost in thought for a while.

Hours passed and it was morning once more. They left the thatched hut and walked to the entrance of the Whining Road again.

Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh! After they passed along the fences, they eagerly advanced through the rolling white mist.

The two rows of fences functioned not only as the entrance but the exit as well.

There were two different worlds on either side of the fences.

Right after the Wing King swiftly soared out of the white mist, they saw a potholed swamp ahead of them.

Most swamps were usually dangerous. No one knew what might be lurking in them. Now, the swamp in front of them was quite peculiar.

Those deep recesses contained blood rather than normal swamp water. It looked a bit horrific.

"Wow. This is the Blood Swamp. It has already expanded so much!" the Snake Goddess exclaimed in surprise. She did not expect it to be quite this expansive.

However, the three Eternal Realm Hunters were not surprised when they saw the Blood Swamp. The expressions on their faces remained impassive.

"The Blood Swamp will expand every thirty years and it will also shrink in another thirty years. Right now it's in the process of expanding. It's normal for it to expand up to the exit of the Whining Road," Pearson chimed in nonchalantly.

Originally, the Eternal Realm Hunters' goal was to hunt down Zen and his group.
