The Wing King closed his eyes and a green light instantly rose above his head.

It didn't matter how far away he was. He could always communicate with the Civilization Artifact of the Regal Jade Civilization any time. His bond to it was quite special. It was almost as though it was a part of his body.

Buzz! Buzz! "The Regal Jade Spirit." The Wing King's voice reached the Civilization Artifact and sounded from it.

Chapter 3997 Running After the Treacherous Being drilled into him, Zen completely lost control of his body.

Like flowing water, the Treacherous Being drilled into every bone in Zen's body, assimilating itself into him.

Fortunately, the Treacherous Being did not invade his soul.

At some point, he ended up in the Blood Swamp.

Splash! Splash! Splash! In its low-lying land, the Blood Swamp lived up to its name. Blood spurted and splashed everywhere.

"Primeval Lord of Heaven, where are we? Why is there blood everywhere?"

Zen asked.

"This is the Blood Swamp," the Primeval Lord of Heaven answered. "It is very dangerous. If you are not careful, you will die here."

For Eternal Realm Hunters who were familiar with the Blood Swamp, this place might not have been so terrifying.

But to those who stumbled into it for the first time, the Blood Swamp was hell.

Underneath the surface of the blood-red puddles, there lived bright red leeches. They camouflaged perfectly with the scarlet blood, and it was difficult even for the spiritual sense to detect them.

Once they quietly latched themselves onto someone, they would release toxins that paralyzed their victims. Then, slowly, those bloodthirsty leeches would devour their victims' souls.

The most terrifying part was that, once they devoured the souls, they would occupy their victims' bodies for a while.

The Soul Leeches didn't have a mind of their own, but they instinctively moved their victims to the Worm Lizards.

The Blood Swamp also had a unique ecosystem.

The Worm Lizard was massive. It was on top of the food chain in the Blood Swamp.

Any creature that had the misfortune of stumbling across the nests of the Worm Lizards would be dragged into the darkness, never to see the light of day again.

However, the Worm Lizards couldn't leave their nests, so their range of movement was limited. Except for those who didn't know much about the Blood Swamp, all the creatures knew to avoid the Worm Lizards' nests.

Therefore, they depended on the Soul Leeches to hunt for them.

However, it was a mutual relationship. The Soul Leeches hunted willingly because they needed the Worm Lizards' blood in order to grow stronger.

As Zen ran haphazardly through the swamp, viscous blood splashed all over him.

The Soul Leeches took this opportunity and quietly latched onto his body.

Slowly, they crawled towards his head.

Although these Soul Leeches were very small, Zen noticed them immediately.

"Primeval Lord of Heaven, there are leeches crawling all over me!" Zen cried.

The Primeval Lord of Heaven was silent for a moment as he studied the situation. "These are the Soul Leeches. They can devour your soul."

"What? These little things can devour my soul?" Zen echoed, his brows furrowing in concern.

"Yes, their abilities are very magical, and they often..." The Primeval Lord of Heaven began to warn Zen, but he had already sprung into action.

"Guess I'll have to get rid of them!"

As he spoke, Zen willed his soul to attack the Soul Leeches.

Since he'd already reached the Holy Soul Realm, his soul was much stronger than that of an ordinary warrior at the Chaotic Source Realm. It wasn't hard for him to slay the leeches that crawled all over his body.

Buzz! Zen's soul glowed dangerously and countless tiny rays of light shot out.

Da! Da! Da! The rays of light turned into small swords which slashed at the Soul Leeches. They didn't stand a chance. In the blink of an eye, the Soul Leeches that latched onto Zen's body were shredded to pieces.

Zen let out a sigh of relief.

However, since he was still running uncontrollably, more blood splashed onto him, and with it, more leeches latched onto his skin. Some leeches even managed to take a bite out of Zen's soul.

Even with the help of nine Holy Soul Imprints, his soul was still unable to withstand the attacks from the Soul Leeches.

Zen winced in pain. He knew he couldn't hold out any longer. So, he willed his soul to retreat back into the depths of his mind.

"These leeches are so powerful!" he whined.

The Soul Leeches had only managed to take a few bites, but he already felt half his soul was paralyzed.

"You didn't let me finish speaking," the Primeval Lord of Heaven reprimanded. "Let Zhurong deal with them."

As soon as he finished speaking, Zhurong appeared above Zen's head.

Zhurong's energy soul was shrouded in flames, which burned over Zen's head. Soon, the flames enveloped Zen's entire body. From afar, he looked like a burning man running desperately.

The Soul Leeches on Zen's body were scorched into nothingness by the flames, and the blood from the swamp evaporated quickly.

That was one problem dealt with. However, he was still being controlled by the Treacherous Being.

By now, the Primeval Lord of Heaven and Zen had already figured out that the Treacherous Being didn't have its own consciousness.

What the Treacherous Being had said when it possessed Zen's body had been deciphered by the Heavenly Obsession Civilization. It was instinctively expressing its regret and anger, trying to break free from the shackles of the Whining Road.

Now it ran like mad, driven solely by instinct.

As for where it was running towards, Zen didn't have the slightest clue.

Neither did he have the time to figure it out, since his top priority now was to stay alive.

Zhurong was just a wisp of energy soul, and before long, his energy was exhausted.

So he was sent back to Zen's inner world. Now, it was Emperor Charm's turn to make a move. After him, another would take his place.

The human heroes had become Zen's bodyguards, protecting his soul from being devoured by the Soul Leeches.

While the many human heroes took turns to attack, Zen's body suddenly stepped into a large pond.

To his surprise, he didn't sink. At the pace he was running, it was a piece of cake for him to walk on the water.

However, he had only taken a few strides forward when a massive head suddenly emerged from the water. It was a Worm Lizard's head. The pond was its nest! Splash! The huge Worm Lizard opened its big mouth and swallowed Zen in one gulp.

It was a creature in the Supreme Pure Realm, so it was far stronger than the creatures in the Grand Pure Realm.

The Worm Lizard had sensed Zen's presence long ago through those Soul Leeches, but it was very disappointed that Zen killed them off so easily.

However, to its delight, Zen came straight to its nest. Such good luck! The Worm Lizard excitedly snapped its mouth shut and was sinking back into the pond when suddenly, cracks as thick as an arm appeared on the surface of its skull.

Crack! Crack! Crack! The cracks rapidly spread, causing the Worm Lizard to feel a little uneasy.

'What's going on here...' it thought confusedly.

When it finally realized that it was the human in its mouth that was causing the cracks, it was too late. Before it could even react, its head exploded into tiny pieces.

Zen emerged, unscathed, and continued sprinting across the pond as though nothing happened.

Chapter 3998 To The North All the creatures hiding throughout the Blood Swamp were shocked by the Worm Lizard's death.

Despite being the dominant creature of the Blood Swamp, the Worm Lizard had easily been shredded from the inside out. This was incomprehensible to the other creatures.

However, these creatures were only momentarily stunned before they swarmed into the nest of the Worm Lizard.

The Worm Lizard was ginormous, and its flesh and blood contained precious substances.

After devouring them, these creatures would be greatly fortified.

How could they miss out on such a rare opportunity? As the blood surged wildly in the pool, the dead Worm Lizard's bones and flesh were rapidly devoured until nothing was left...

Splatter...

The Treacherous Beings were lethal. Sometimes they appeared quite docile, but at other times they became extremely violent.

Therefore, no one knew how they came into being or how they had disappeared. Even though they had wanted to study them, they had no idea where to begin.

Many people viewed the Treacherous Beings as souls of the Instant Civilization. As to why these souls couldn't communicate with them or why they acted so unpredictably, there was no explanation for this either.

"That is feasible. However, I was just wondering where this Treacherous Being will lead me to..." Zen sighed with resignation.

After the Blood Swamp's expansion, it now occupied a massive area and seemed almost endless.

What replaced them in the food chain was an even more ferocious creature, the Swamp Prawn.

The Swamp Prawns possessed an astonishingly hard outer shell and congregated in large numbers. They usually hunted in packs and could instantly devour their prey.

Chapter 3999 The Same Direction "It's heading for the Myriad Pagoda Mountains in the north. What a great coincidence!" Zen exclaimed. "I wonder what it is going to do there." The Jade Pure Realm was the core area among the Three Purities Stage, and also the most mysterious one.

Like the Element Spirit Civilization, almost all civilizations also wanted to enter and explore what was inside the Jade Pure Realm. That being said, the human race was no exception.

"Wait a minute. So you mean that the entrance to the Jade Pure Realm is in that direction?" Zen was utterly shocked.

The Primeval Lord of Heaven smiled bitterly. "Well, why do you think we're trapped in here in the first place?"

It turned out that all of the thirty-nine human heroes were trapped on their way to the Jade Pure Realm.

The entrance to the Jade Pure Realm had been a tremendous secret for most of the civilizations.

As the Primeval Lord of Heaven led the human race into the Three Purities Stage, the search for the way to the Jade Pure Realm had always been their top priority.

The entrance to the Supreme Pure Realm was located at the center of the Grand Pure Realm. So, the assumption was that the entrance to the Jade Pure Realm might be also lying at the center of the Supreme Pure Realm.

Based on this conjecture, the Primeval Lord of Heaven had managed to find some clues and ultimately discovered an underground passage at the back of the Myriad Pagoda Mountains.

"Until now, I'm still not a hundred percent sure that the underground passage really leads to the Jade Pure Realm," the Primeval Lord of Heaven said in a disgruntled tone. "But ever since we discovered that passage, the Element Spirit Civilization had launched an all-out attack on us. If that passage was useless, then why were they desperately hindering us?"

At that time, the 77th chaotic era dominated by humans had been destroyed, and the 78th chaotic era had already begun.

Under the leadership of the Primeval Lord of Heaven, the human race began to rise rapidly on the Other Shore. For a very long time, they had been fiercely fighting against the Element Spirit Civilization.

Back then, the Nihility race had yet to come into being, and the human race was the only force that could stand up as near equals to the Element Spirit Civilization.

The Element Spirit Civilization had regarded the human race as a thorn in its flesh and did all it could to restrain their development. However, it never solely focused on them. After all, the Element Spirit Civilization had more than one enemy. Several ruling civilizations had already appeared before the 77th chaos, and these ruling civilizations were also a threat to them.

However, when the Primeval Lord of Heaven had finally led the human race to the underground passage that could possibly lead to the Jade Pure Realm, the Element Spirit Civilization snapped and didn't hold back anymore. They started attacking them with the determination of eradicating the entire race.

"The Eye Spirit gathered almost all of their elite members, but the best that they could do was trap us within the passage," the Primeval Lord of Heaven said with pride.

"If they resorted to these kinds of actions, then they really must have been hiding something important. The passage might be leading to the Jade Pure Realm all along," Zen affirmed.

"Well, that's why I said that I'm still not a hundred percent sure. There are just too many secrets in the Three Purities Stage, and the Element Spirit Civilization came before everyone else, so they must have uncovered most of these secrets. They destroyed those without much value, hid the important ones, and tried to keep them to themselves. Anyway, whether it leads to the Jade Pure Realm or not, I'm sure that the Element Spirit Civilization wants to hide something from us, that's why they kept us from advancing in that underground passage." The Primeval Lord of Heaven's words carried the weight of his determination.

While he was communicating with the Primeval Lord of Heaven through his mind, Zen also looked around and examined his surroundings at the same time.

He saw that the Myriad Pagoda Mountains covered a very large area.

The mountains here were completely different from the other mountainous areas.

At a glance, every mountain looked like a lofty pagoda.

Moreover, it was an amazing sight to behold that all of the mountains were almost of the same height and shape.

As he passed through them, he felt as if he had entered a strange, immense forest formed by numerous lofty mountains.

"I just had an idea. Although the Treacherous Being doesn't seem to possess much intelligence, it knows Sanskrit words. How about we try communicating with it?" Zen suggested.

The Primeval Lord of Heaven had long established a capable team within Zen's inner world. This team was well-trained and it would be easy for them to pronounce even the complicated Sanskrit words.

After getting out of the Whining Road, Zen had been preoccupied with the constant troubles that he encountered in the Blood Swamp.

The Myriad Pagoda Mountains looked much quieter and safer, so he deemed it to be a good chance to give it a try.

The Primeval Lord of Heaven had also originally planned to do the same thing, but the situation didn't permit him.

Thus, when Zen suggested it, he quickly gathered the members of his team.

They had practiced and made other preparations to be skilled in terms of cooperation and synchronization.

Following the instructions of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization, they began to pronounce the corresponding Sanskrit words. Their voices echoed in Zen's body.

"Can you understand me? Who are you? Can you communicate with me?"

As they pronounced the Sanskrit words together, their voices eventually formed a rhythmic song.

The Treacherous Being had taken over Zen's entire body, so it should be able to hear the song.

Both Zen and the Primeval Lord of Heaven waited expectantly for the Treacherous Being to respond.

However, to their dismay, it only continued to control Zen's body by running wildly, as if it didn't hear anything at all.

Although the result wasn't totally unexpected, the two of them still felt a little disappointed.

"We could still try a few more times," Zen insisted.

With that, the team in his inner world began chanting again and conveyed the messages through rhythmic songs over and over.

Within five minutes, they repeated the same set of questions multiple times.

However, they still didn't get a single response from the Treacherous Being.

"Well, we did what we could." Zen finally gave up and sighed in disappointment.

It was upsetting enough for him to have his body manipulated by another creature. But what made it worse was that the particular creature didn't have a shred of intelligence.

As Zen chose to give up, he noticed that the Treacherous Being suddenly controlled his body and turned left. It was the first time that the Treacherous Being changed directions after a long while.

After entering the range of the Myriad Pagoda Mountains, it headed north for quite a distance before finally changing directions.

While Zen's expression was more of confusion, the Primeval Lord of Heaven's reaction was the opposite. He was surprised, but there was a huge trace of expectation on his face.

Perceiving this, Zen couldn't help but ask, "What's the matter?" The Primeval Lord of Heaven's reaction just made Zen more confused.

"Listen. The underground passage at the back of the Myriad Pagoda Mountains is not easy to find. It took us nearly a third of the chaotic era just to figure out the way to open it. The direction to get to the passage is to go north for three thousand miles, go west for five thousand miles, and then overturn the largest mountain at sight!" the Primeval Lord of Heaven explained in detail.

Since entering the Myriad Pagoda Mountains, the Primeval Lord of Heaven had paid special attention to the movements of Zen's physical body because of his hunch.

To his surprise, the Treacherous Being had gone north for exactly three thousand miles before it finally turned west.

At the back of the Primeval Lord of Heaven's mind, this didn't seem to be a coincidence anymore.

"Then, perhaps, the Treacherous Being is actually heading for the underground passage that leads to the Jade Pure Realm!" Zen exclaimed in excitement.

'If that's the case, things would definitely work out, ' he thought to himself.

Once they entered the underground passage and met the real selves of the human heroes, they might be able to figure out a way to resolve Zen's current state.

"Well, there's nothing we could do now but hope for the best," the Primeval Lord of Heaven said.

The Myriad Pagoda Mountains was indeed a peaceful area. They didn't encounter any obstacles as Zen's body trod all the way to the west.

It wasn't long before a round pagoda-shaped mountain finally appeared on their view.

The mountain was several times broader than the rest, and it was also much higher.

After arriving at the bottom of the huge mountain, the Treacherous Being paused for a moment before it manipulated Zen's body to climb up the cliff.

As Zen and the Primeval Lord of Heaven witnessed this, their minds were both filled with anticipation.
